Northeast Army

Orders Full-Line Pursuit 81

Wen Nianzhong Discusses Shi's Army's Loss of One-Fifth

Most of the Northeast Army Pursues the Enemy to the Border of Shandong

A letter recently received from the Ping-Han Railway front states that the Northeast Army issued a general attack order on the morning of the 31st of last month. Yu Xuezhong himself departed from Baoding to supervise the troops, stationed at Fangshun Bridge, two stations away from Baoding. From Fangshun Bridge north to Baoding and south to Wangdu, transportation vehicles travel back and forth three times a day to transport military supplies and transmit news. However, important orders are still transmitted by telephone. After the military headquarters special train arrived at Fangshun Bridge, engineers installed a long-distance telephone on the train. According to front-line intelligence, Shi's army failed in the battle of Ranzhuang and retreated automatically. Most of its eastern route concentrated along the Hutuo River via Dongtinglun, and the central route bypassed Shijiazhuang along Zhengding. Another part of the army launched a fierce attack on Tang County west of the railway, attempting to contain the retreat of the central and left routes. The Northeast Army immediately dispatched the 18th Brigade of Du Jiwu to take charge of the left flank and the 14th Brigade of Chen Guanqun to take charge of the central route, respectively pursuing the enemy. Another 30th Brigade of Yu Zhaolin laid siege to Tang County with one part and approached Shijiazhuang along the railway with another part. The plane departed very early one day, and by the evening, it had dropped four reports. According to the reports, Shi Yun's army's baggage vehicles were discovered south of Zhengding. Many bombs were dropped and hit the targets. As for the official Shi's army, most of them retreated, and only a few plainclothes teams remained on the front line, showing slight resistance. The direction of Shi's army's retreat seemed to be toward the southeast. It was heard that the Central Army had intercepted them in the Nangong and Jixian areas, and the Second Army and the First Army were in contact to carry out a pursuit on the flanks and rear of Shi's army. As a result of the continuous pursuit, many prisoners were captured and transported to the rear. One day, two military flags, eleven artillery pieces, and countless rifles were captured. However, when Shi's army retreated, they destroyed the railway south of Qingfengdian. The first train of the Northeast armored train has gone to that area to repair it. Another day, a telegram from the front reported at night that the Northeast Army had occupied Dingzhou at 9:00 PM and was continuing to advance. At the same time, on the 29th and 30th evenings, due to the fierce fighting on the front line, there were many casualties on both sides. There is currently a train full of wounded soldiers being transported to the rear. Broken limbs and bones were a tragic sight. It was heard that most of them were soldiers from the 18th, 14th, 11th, and 3rd brigades. The battle of Ranzhuang was fought by the above three brigades, who tried their best to resist and prevent Shi's army from advancing. Otherwise, Baoding would not have been defended. Therefore, the casualties of these three brigades were higher than those of other units. It was heard that on the evening of the 30th, Shi's army used five brigades to advance back and forth, advancing and retreating three times. The battle was extremely fierce. Therefore, the sound of artillery in Baoding was very clear that night. However, Shi's army benefited from a quick battle and was difficult to defeat quickly, so they retreated. The Deputy Commander commended the brigade commanders of the three brigades for their effective command, which was able to defeat the strong enemy. Reporter recently met with Chief of Staff Wen Nianzhong, who said that our army has issued a full-line pursuit order. The 18th Brigade of Du Jiwu and the 11th Brigade of Dong Yingbin are pursuing the enemy in the An Guo and Shenze areas on the left flank. The 14th Brigade of Chen Guanyi is advancing towards Xinle. The 6th Cavalry Brigade of Bai Fengxiang is approaching the north bank of the Hutuo River. The 4th and 5th Cavalry Brigades of the Jin-Pu Railway have copied out in front of Shi's army to intercept them. A part of the Central Army has gone to Wuqiang Hengshui. This battle was a success of our army's tactics. Shi's army originally had three divisions, which were later expanded to five divisions. In addition, there was a special brigade. Due to insufficient manpower, many civilians were captured in various counties, so there were more than 70,000 people. The loss this time was less than one-fifth. Our army is determined to pursue the enemy with all its strength, in order to eliminate the remnants and eliminate future troubles. On the 2nd, Yu Xuezhong sent a telegram to take office as the commander of the First Group Army of the Northern Route Suppression of the Red Army, and specially made a military flag, which was red with three stars, which was extremely bright. On the same day, Yu arrived at Wangdu from Fangshun Bridge. Reporter met Yu at the station, who said that he would not stop here, but would abandon the railway and start to advance on land to supervise the pursuit between Dingzhou and Anguo, and then to Shenze. The enemy is now retreating to the southeast. Our army is determined to unite with all armies to intercept them, but only to the border of Shandong. It is expected to be completed in a week. Most of our army does not enter Shijiazhuang, but only a part of the 30th Brigade advances from the Ping-Han front. When our headquarters arrives at the Shandong border, if there are no other problems, it may change to the Jin-Pu Railway to return to Ping. But at this moment, the first step in the solution to Shi's army is to intercept it, in order to divide its military strength, so that it will not remain united, causing future troubles. Now the Central and Northeast armies have advanced. If it is absolutely necessary, order Shi's army to flee into Shandong. Our army's advance and retreat will be subject to the orders of the Central Committee, but there must be a proper solution. As for Shunde, it was heard that there was still a part of Shi's army in the city to defend it. The northward advance of the Central Army, it was heard, was to bypass the left and right routes. In the future, when the majority of Shi's army is resolved, then that part will naturally not be a problem, or it may flee into the nearby mountains, it is also unknown. As for the situation in the front, according to the plane report obtained today, Shi's army was discovered along the Hutuo River. Two bombs were dropped by the plane, and both were hit. The other side suffered heavy casualties and suffered great losses. (2nd)

Shao Lizi Returns to Beijing 82

Fan Pujiang Arrives in Jinan to Discuss the Resolution of Shi's Remnants

A Jinan announcement states that Shao Lizi, the Secretary-General of the Land, Sea, and Air Force Headquarters, came to Jinan by order of the Central Committee to discuss with Han Fuju, the chairman of the Shandong Provincial Government, how to deal with Shi Yousan. Now that Shi's army has been resolved, and Shandong is as calm as ever, Shao is returning to Beijing to report. The unfinished task here will be handled by Jiang Bocheng and Han in close contact. Therefore, Shao, along with his wife and secretary Peng Xuehuan, took the Pingpu No. 201 train back to Beijing this morning. At 8:00 AM this morning, Shao first went to the provincial government to say goodbye. Han then kept Shao for breakfast and made final consultations on the measures to accept Shi's army. After breakfast, Shao, along with his wife, Chairman Han, his wife, Education Director He Siyuan, Agriculture and Mining Director Wang Fangting, Construction Director Zhang Honglie, Finance Director Wang Xiangrong, Provincial Secretary-General Zhang Shaotang, Salt Transport Envoy Yuan Lichen, etc., left the provincial government by car to the station. All the way from the provincial government to the station, the guards were increased. Inside the platform, Yang Xigeng, the deputy head of the pistol brigade's second regiment, led a company of soldiers to guard and escort them. Those who came to the station to see them off included Jiang Bocheng and his wife, Deputy Commander Zhang's representative Ge Guangting, Civil Affairs Director Li Shuchun, Jinan Mayor Wen Chenglie, and Public Security Director Wang Kairu. When Shao arrived at the station, the train had not yet arrived, so Shao waited in the lounge. At that time, Shao told reporters that Chairman Han upheld justice and acted as a pillar in the middle of the river to solve the problem of Shi's army. Therefore, it was able to be resolved in the shortest possible time, making the situation in the north safe again. The results of this visit were satisfactory, and Commander-in-Chief Jiang and Deputy Commander Zhang were very satisfied. Now that Shi's army is no longer a problem, Yu may go to Nanchang after Beijing to report the process to the Commander-in-Chief, but it is still not certain. Han Fuju also told reporters that Shi's army is now retreating to Shenze. The Central Committee ordered Yu to be responsible for accepting Shi's army, and he will of course comply with the order. However, the distance is too far, and Shi's army may not actually flee to Shandong. Even if he comes, Yu will welcome him, because the main force of Shi is the Sun Guangqian and Mi Wenhe troops, which are of good quality. If Shi comes in person, as long as he leaves the team, Commander-in-Chief Jiang is magnanimous and will definitely protect his personal safety. As for the troops newly collected by Shi, most of them are bandits and their discipline is too bad. If they come to Shandong, they will definitely harass the local people, which Yu will not welcome. Now we have made full preparations for accepting Shi's army, and we will further explore the trends of Shi's army and deal with them temporarily. It was also said that the issue of clearing the countryside in Shandong and Henan is currently being planned. The Pingpu No. 201 train then entered the station, and Deputy Zhang's representative Fan Pujiang took the car to Jinan. The important people first welcomed Mr. Fan, and then sent Shao on the train. According to Fan, the mission of this visit was to report the battle between the Northeast Army and Shi Yousan's army to Chairman Han on behalf of the Deputy Commander, and to bring the Deputy Commander's handwritten letter, which stated that if a small number of Shi's troops fled into Shandong, please Chairman Han be responsible for resolving the issue to avoid disturbing the local people. Shi's army is now fleeing southeast from Shulu, and most of them have crossed the Hutuo River. There were no major losses on both sides in this battle. Because the Deputy Commander advocated peace and did not want to start a war, he retreated to Shijiazhuang, then to Zhengding, and then to Wangdu. It was hoped that Shi would finally realize his mistake. Shi's army advanced step by step, forcing them to more than ten miles away from Baoding. The Deputy Commander believed that the opportunity was imminent and could not retreat any further. The conflicts began with Shi's army, and the soldiers were fortunate enough to be able to solve it quickly, without causing great chaos in the local area. It was fortunate. At that time, Shao Lizi talked with Fan, and Shao asked whether Shi's army had fled to southern Shanxi. Fan replied that there was none, and said that most of the artillery of Shi's army was lost. The Second Army Commander of the Northeast Army, Wang Shuchang, has withdrawn to Machang from the front line, but the cavalry is still in the front line to intercept Shi's army. The whereabouts of Shi Yousan are still unknown. When it was ten o'clock, the car arrived and started. Shao Lizi and his wife boarded the car, and Han and Fan Pujiang Ge Guangting Jiang Bocheng went to the provincial government to meet and hosted a banquet for Fan. (August 4th)

A Record of Inspecting Fresh Cases (Continued) 83

A Brief Account of Korean Customs and Topography: In the North and South Pyeongan Provinces, the Gyeonggi, Hwanghae, and Gangwon Provinces of Korea, mountain ranges stretch continuously and endlessly, without vast plains or wilderness. Only the basins of the Daedong River and the Jin River have relatively lower terrain. Because the Hwanghae Province is close to the coast, the land is still fertile and agricultural products are abundant. The other provinces rely solely on the two water sources of the Daedong and Jin Rivers to divert water to grow rice. The main agricultural product is rice, followed by sorghum and soybeans. Grains are also planted occasionally. The population is extremely dense, with a large village every one or two li. Due to the population, the fields of the wealthy are at most 100 square feet, with each square foot being six feet square. Ordinary families cultivate only four or five square feet. There are many people who are alone and rely on their own strength. The only way to maintain a livelihood is to work hard. Therefore, the majority of the people in Korea are laborers. Most ordinary people do not engage in production. Those with land rent it out to others and live off the rent. Men sit indoors all day long, drinking alcohol from large bowls, or seeking two or three companions to play chess in the mountains and forests, spending their leisurely and happy years, regardless of drought, flood, or chaos. The poor are hired to work for others, but they are often unwilling to work hard, and the rewards they receive are used to consume liquor. In each city, town, and village, there are no places to sell drinks. The only places available are the restaurants that sell alcohol. There are two types of alcohol. The expensive one is like the old wine of our country, and the inferior one is like rice water, the color of horse urine. Usually, five cents (Japanese money) buys a bowl. Koreans who are traveling or working and thirsty buy several bowls and drink them like cattle. The wine is called "Makgeolli." The reporter once bought and tasted it. It tastes bitter and slightly salty, and its turbidity is nauseating. I don't know why Koreans are so fond of it. Koreans do not save. There is no overnight food in the house, even among the wealthy. Every day after breakfast, men and women go back and forth to the towns and villages, either carrying a pot or a bag. All of them are buying food. Most of their time is spent on this. The lack of value of time is most evident among Koreans. Those who live in Sinuiju cross the river to Andong every day to buy food. They travel more than ten li back and forth, running under the scorching sun, without considering it a hardship. It is truly a strange thing. Most of the houses of ordinary families are made of thatched grass and mud, and the architecture is extremely poor, all the same, without any new patterns. The rooms are short, and one must bend over to enter. Facing the door is an earthen kang, and the stove is located at one end, dug into the ground without piling it up. When burning, the room is filled with thick smoke, but those who drink and play chess are calm in the room, without diminishing their interest. The more well-off wealthy families, or those listed in the gentry class, cover the roof with tiles, and carve wood into lattices. Inside the room, there is a front room, an outer room, and an inner room. Family members rest in the inner room, and do not come out even when guests arrive, which strictly separates men and women. Most of the food is millet (grain). Although rice is produced, they do not grind it themselves. Guests

Overseas Chinese Children in Incheon 84

They consider cold noodles to be a superior dish. The method involves pounding rice into noodles, pressing them through a sieve-like device to create thin strands, and then boiling them before putting them into cold water. They are combined with sour and spicy ingredients and are even given as a supreme gift. However, when we [Chinese] eat it, even those who have lived in Korea for a long time frown and find it hard to swallow. Very few are engaged in commerce. If they do business at all, they only sell rice and cloth. Their shops are generally crude and small, with goods piled haphazardly on earthen platforms. The so-called clerks, shop assistants, managers, and boss's wives sit around in the room, leaning against the goods, playing chess or drinking wine. When tired, they lean back against the piles of goods and take a nap. Even when customers come, they barely open their eyes to look and do not bother to serve them, continuing their dream journeys. This fundamentally deprives them of the ability to compete with our fellow overseas Chinese. Therefore, hardly one in a hundred Koreans engages in business profitably. There are two styles of marriage, new and old. The new style is mostly practiced by young students, with simple wedding and engagement procedures, often held in a church. The old style is largely like ours in China, except that the woman keeps her eyes tightly shut from the moment she gets into the sedan until she arrives at her husband's home, forbidden to open them, otherwise it is considered inauspicious. The concept of female chastity is not as strict as before, and there are many free marriages. For both men and women, clothing styles have remained the same for hundreds of years. In summer, they all wear white summer cloth. Women's clothing, with an upper garment and lower skirt, follows the ancient system. However, in the capital [Seoul], skirts are still light green; in Pyongyang, still black; and in other places, still white. Men's trousers are particularly baggy, allowing them to retract their heads into the trousers at night, as if in a bag, sleeping soundly without fear of mosquito bites. This is also a special system. Although overseas Chinese have lived in Korea for a long time, very few marry Korean women. It is not that Chinese and Koreans cannot intermarry, but rather that once a Korean woman is married, her relatives come to bother them every day, either staying for a long time or leaving and returning. Entertaining and treating them is a small matter, but providing gifts upon their departure is hard to sustain. If there are no gifts, they take and carry things away themselves, without the host's consent. If the supply is not maintained, then they have no choice but to divorce. The old Korean palace in the capital, now a relic of the fallen dynasty, has been converted by the Japanese into Changgyeongwon Park, divided into botanical and zoological gardens and a museum. The palace architecture resembles the Manchu Qing palaces of Shengjing [Mukden]. All Korean relics, stone coffins, sarcophagi, Buddhist sutras, pottery, and clothing, are displayed inside. Many Japanese, Korean, and Chinese people visit. The zoo's collection is particularly rich, with lions, elephants, tigers, leopards, walruses, crocodiles, and other species, amounting to more than a dozen kinds, representing a large-scale animal collection. There are no bandits anywhere in Korea. People do not lock their doors at night, and no one picks up lost items on the road. This is ostensibly due to the power of Japanese politics, but in reality, even though Koreans are so poor they don't even have a foothold, they also lack the courage to resort to desperate measures.

Continued Report on the Wuhan Flood 87

Tens of Thousands of Refugees in Hankou After Four Days of Flooding

Dikes Along the Riverbank in Wuchang Are in Danger of Breaching

A dispatch from Hankou states that after the Dan Shuichi dike and the railway tunnel gate successively breached, Hankou was completely flooded. After four days, the people have been displaced and uprooted. The misery is too dreadful to witness. On the Wuchang side, the Sai Hu dike and the Xu Jia Peng riverbank are also showing signs of danger and may not last. The authorities are trying to take care of both sides and are overwhelmed. We, the remaining survivors, can only await death with our hands tied. I, as one of the refugees, witnessed this flood and was unable to prevent the catastrophe. I will write down the tragedy of the Wuhan disaster and the suffering of the people, and proclaim it to the whole country, hoping that those who care about the disaster in Hubei will hear about it.

Hankou area On the second day, at 12:00 noon, floodwaters poured into Hankou, flooding the entire city. On the third, fourth, and fifth days, the water level has not receded slightly. In higher-lying areas, the water is more than a foot or several feet deep. In low-lying areas, it is as deep as twenty feet. People are supporting the old and carrying the young, sheltering in the water, and some are squatting on rooftops. Most of the government employees are staying in hotels, or traveling back and forth in the city by car or boat. The contrast is quite striking, with some enjoying luxury and others in misery. When the flood first arrived, people did not have time to escape, and many died. The area where the Dan Shuichi tunnel gate breached suffered especially heavy casualties. Every day, about two to three hundred corpses are found, often tied together with straw ropes. The corpses of pigs and cows are everywhere, which is also miserable. The exact number of dead and injured has not yet been investigated, but the number of refugees has reached 220,000, or even more than that. The Flood Relief Association has expanded the refugee shelters to eight locations and has added 20 staff members to the relief section, with Huang Wenzhi as the director-general and Cai Fuqing and others as staff members, to engage in relief work. The city party headquarters and the Second Bandit Suppression Propaganda Office have also organized a慰问队to purchase food and medicine and transport them by boat to distribute in the disaster area. Major shops and charitable organizations have also organized rescue teams to provide relief in different directions. Initially, prices rose more than double. After the commander of the military camp strictly prohibited it, prices have decreased slightly. There is a great shortage of grain and rice. Chairman He Chengjun has telegraphed General Commander Jiang [Chiang Kai-shek] and Chairman Lu Dipin of Jiangxi to purchase 100,000 piculs of rice in Jiangxi to transport to Hankou for relief. In terms of public security, thanks to the effective maintenance of the military and police, it is still stable. In addition to the original garrison troops, more than eight additional battalions have been dispatched to control the area near Wuhan. On one hand, the military camp has issued instructions to its subordinates to investigate criminals and prevent riots, and has established four measures: (1) Local officials and gentry should conduct a household census in their respective jurisdictions, and any new arrivals to hotels without guarantors should be expelled; (2) Strictly prevent petty thieves and pay attention to normally restless vagrants; (3) Local jurisdictions where disturbances occur will result in punishment of officials and gentry; (4) Government employees should go to their offices to work and not stay in hotels. As for the accumulated water in Hankou, 20,000 yuan has been allocated on the fifth to build a long embankment from Minquan Road to the Japanese concession, using machines to drain the water out. It is scheduled to start construction on the sixth and drain the water by the tenth. However, when planning to drain the street water, the embankments at Qiaokou, Huangjingtang, Pizi Street, and the Pacific Soap Factory became critical again. He Chengjun has ordered the mayor of Hankou, He Baohua, and the director of the Water Conservancy Bureau, Chen Keming, to find ways to carry out emergency repairs. If there is another breach, they will be held accountable. It is reported that He and Chen have already been attacked for their ineffective rescue efforts and failure to carry out repairs when the Dan Shuichi breach occurred, and He has also been impeached by the provincial and city party headquarters. Now that they have received this strict order, they know that they cannot delay any longer, so the footsteps of the two have already been seen at Qiaokou, Huangjingtang, and other places in recent days.

Wuchang area The terrain of Wuchang is slightly higher than that of Hankou. After Hankou was flooded, many disaster victims crossed the river to seek refuge, all regarding it as paradise. Unexpectedly, after the Wuqing Gate embankment breached, the water inside the Wutai Gate was also level with the Wuqing Gate, gradually threatening to inundate this majestic city. On the fourth day, Zhengjie Street outside the Baoan Gate was flooded by three feet, and Shoushan Temple Street, Sai Bao Alley, and Minglun Street were all flooded. At the same time, the Sai Hu dike and the Xu Jia Peng riverbank outside the Tongxiang Gate were in extreme danger. Fang Dazhi, the director of the Construction Department, went to inspect after hearing the news and ordered the blockade of Pinghu Gate, Yuecheng two city gates and the lake, the Wenchang Gate city gate cave and culvert, the Wangshan Gate city gate and culvert, the Qing Shiqiao culvert, the Xiaodongcheng, the Dadongmen South Radio Station, the Renhui Bridge, Shisiying, Yunjia Bridge, Tanhualin, Wusheng Gate, and other culverts one after another. The Mada Gate ditch and the total drainage ditch outside the Tongxiang Gate are currently flowing outward. Once blocked, the water will accumulate in the city, so the ditch mouths are lined with burlap sacks, and they will be blocked only when necessary. According to those who know the terrain well, reinforcing the embankments and blocking the ditches is only a temporary solution. For a foolproof plan, the bridge holes in the Tongxiang Gate area should be blocked as soon as possible, and a long embankment should be added between the Changchun Temple and the railway. Sandbags should also be used to build an embankment in the Bowen College, Dongyue Temple area, so that even if the Sai Hu dike collapses, Wuchang can be safe. According to the personnel guarding the Sai Hu dike, the embankment protection project is not large, but they are suffering from the lack of necessary materials, and sometimes they are at a loss as to what to do. For example, in the middle section where the water cave is leaking, there is a lack of wooden piles, and the leaking water continues to seep in, which is very distressing. This situation is indeed real, because the Hubei province's dike funds have been embezzled by local merchants. At a time when the provincial treasury is extremely tight, how can there be surplus funds to allocate? The authorities cannot shirk their responsibility.

Aftermath measures The Flood Relief Association, considering the seriousness of the disaster, has formulated four aftermath measures and jointly issued a notice with the provincial government yesterday, which reads: "Considering that the flood in our province this time is extremely serious, unprecedented since the Daoguang era of the Qing Dynasty, the rivers and streams have risen together, and the dikes have collapsed. All counties have suffered the same devastation, and the provincial towns have become swamps. The people are displaced and flock to Wuhan, where the summer heat is oppressive, scorching above and humid below. They are perched precariously, and it is difficult to find a full meal. The sight is heartbreaking. Our government and association are aware of the catastrophe and the hardship of the times. We are now proposing plans to help the people in need and have decided on the following four measures: (1) Resettling the displaced. There are many refugees in this flood. In the suburbs of Wuhan alone, according to the survey reports, on both sides of the river, inside and outside the railway, from Wuqing Gate to Dan Shuichi, there are valleys and pits filled with people crying out for food. If we do not immediately take measures to resettle them, they will inevitably be stranded and become even more displaced. In addition to repeatedly sending letters and orders to the Hankou Municipal Government, the Public Security Bureau, the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau, the Wuchang County Office, and social organizations to repeatedly inspect and provide relief at any time, Chengjun and others have also personally inspected the area to formulate a comprehensive plan. At present, in Wuchang, the yarn, cloth, silk, and hemp four bureaus outside Wenchang Gate and the Kai Zi camp and other places have been selected for resettlement. In Hankou, the Charity Association, Wanshou Palace, Xinshi Marketplace, Xinhua Company, Changsha Guildhall, and various hotels have been selected for resettlement. For those who are floating on the water, the association has hired many ships, selected staff members, and planted flags and signs to guide them to the designated locations for rest. (2) Relieving the famine. Once the disaster victims have a place to stay, we should rush to provide relief. It is found that there is nothing better to relieve hunger than cooking porridge, and cooking porridge requires rice. In this flood, rice prices have skyrocketed. In the emergency relief, we must separately arrange cooking porridge and selling rice at low prices according to the urgency and priority. Regarding the matter of cooking porridge, in Wuchang, disaster victim certificates have been prepared. Those who are verified to be genuine will be temporarily issued three yuan per household. It is also planned to separately sell 160,000 piculs of rice at low prices to relieve the market and maintain the people's food supply. With supply and demand in balance, both the gentry and the refugees will receive real benefits. (3) Preventing the spread of epidemics. After a major disaster, there are bound to be many epidemics. The old and weak are gathered together, and if one person dies suddenly, germs will spread everywhere. Therefore, preventing epidemics is listed after resettling the displaced as the most important task in disaster relief. In addition to sending letters to the provincial and municipal hospitals, assigning doctors to carry medicines and go to the resettlement centers to provide treatment at any time, the association will also organize a rescue team to inspect the disaster victims and provide emergency aid. As for the remains of those who died suddenly or drowned, the association will collect and bury them to promote humanity and hygiene. (4) Urgently seeking to restore transportation. The flood situation in Hankou is more severe, and there are more households. All transportation issues are particularly important. In recent days, there have been reports of people being electrocuted to death due to water damage to electrical wires, and people falling into the water and dying due to missteps. In addition to requesting the water and electricity company to quickly prevent all dangerous situations where electric shock may occur, the municipal government and the Public Security Bureau are also hiring small boats to facilitate travel. Once the flood recedes slightly, dredging will be carried out. In addition, the government and association will both deliberate on any matters that can serve as a warning for the future and should be carefully planned to ensure a comprehensive plan. As for the disaster situation in various outer counties, we have separately compiled tables to investigate and clarify the truth in order to determine the relief measures. We have also sent telegrams to the county magistrates of various counties to first organize emergency relief and not allow the disaster victims to be scattered and helpless. However, at a time when there are many incidents in the suburbs and the lives of the people are hanging by a thread, looking to the future only increases our vigilance and trepidation. We hope that kind people and gentlemen will either list the advantages and disadvantages, or donate grain and distribute it, or give medicine and clothes, each doing their best to make up for the shortcomings and save the situation. Everything depends on cooperation. In addition to issuing separate orders, we urgently issue this joint notice, hoping that everyone will be fully informed." (August 5th)

The Tragic Situation of the Flood in Wuxue 88

A dispatch from Wuxue states that since July 10th, there has been continuous heavy rain, accompanied by thunder and lightning, and the weather has been unusually cool. For two weeks now, the river water has risen sharply, and the main wharves, such as the Lower City Main Street, the River Street, the New Street, and the Shangguan, Xiaguan, and Chengzu Streets, are all flooded by three to four feet of water. Commerce has therefore come to a standstill. Currently, large and small shops are moving to other locations, causing house prices to skyrocket, increasing by two-thirds compared to normal rental prices. Yesterday, a section of the official embankment in Erfu Street suddenly leaked. Fortunately, the dike watchmen discovered it and reported it to various agencies, which gathered nearby farmers to collect tools for blocking the water and urgently built a temporary earthen dam. They worked through the night in the rain to temporarily prevent any further damage. However, there are also three or four places in the upper and lower official dams that seem quite dangerous. The people are all in a state of extreme panic. Moreover, the water level in the inland lakes has increased even more. Guangwu Auto has been blocked by the water, and ships have also completely stopped running. As a result, the livelihoods of the dockworkers at various stations have been affected, and the company's losses have also been enormous. In addition, the Weiyi Dam in Luocheng reported four dangerous spots the day before yesterday. Villagers have been working day and night to carry out emergency repairs, but despite using wooden rafts and large trees to block the leaks, there has been no effect, so it has already breached. Furthermore, Guangji County, which is a major producer of grain and rice, is said to have been flooded, and the prospects for cotton, hemp, and tobacco in other places are also hopeless. It is reported that this major disaster is unprecedented in decades. The entire county is in a state of panic over food supplies. Moreover, after suffering from banditry for years, they are now facing a devastating flood, so the people's livelihoods in the future are a cause for serious concern.

After the Cheluo Dam Was Opened, A New Dam Was Opened Again 89

The Nanguan Dam Was Also Secretly Opened

Refugee Shelters Have Been Set Up in Gaoyou City

A dispatch from Gaoyou on the 3rd states that the water level of the Grand Canal in Gaoyou has been rising continuously in recent days. As of yesterday (2nd), it has risen to one zhang, eight chi, and eight cun. The Gaoyou office of the Jiangsu Water Conservancy Bureau received a telegram from the provincial government at 2:00 AM yesterday, ordering the opening of the dam. It also ordered Camp Commander Wang, stationed in Yang, to bring his troops to Gaoyou to assist. After receiving the telegram, Director Mao immediately sent a letter to Magistrate Wang, asking him to dispatch a police team, a Gaobao You patrol team, and the Public Security Bureau to assemble at 5:00 AM yesterday to open the Cheluo Dam. The farmers from the five lower counties who were protecting the dam jumped into the Grand Canal upon seeing the police team approaching to open the dam. Fortunately, they were all rescued and did not drown. At that time, the county magistrates and representatives of various counties also rushed to the scene by boat and consulted with Director Mao. If the water rose again today, the dam would be opened. In the end, both sides sent people to inspect the water level. Upon receiving the report that the water had not increased or decreased, they ordered the police teams to return to the city first. At 3:00 PM, the county party headquarters convened an emergency meeting of various agencies in the county. Suddenly, a telephone report came from Nanmen, stating that the southwest wind had suddenly picked up at this time, the river water had risen sharply, and the canal embankment was in extreme danger. Magistrate Wang immediately joined the county magistrates of various counties, Director Mao of the Water Conservancy Bureau, and the military police and provincial water police stationed in Youcheng to go to open the dam by boat. The farmers protecting the dam stepped forward to prevent the police team from landing. While they were arguing, Camp Commander Wang arrived with his troops to assist, and the dam was finally opened. At that time, there were only over 300 farmers protecting the dam. The thousands of other farmers had heard earlier that the water level could be maintained up to two zhang and thought that the dam would not be opened for the time being, so they had all returned to their villages to harvest rice. After the dam was opened, the farmers protecting the dam all went home in tears, a very tragic sight. At that time, rumors suddenly spread throughout the city, claiming that farmers in Xinghua had dug up the head sluice gates along the river and were planning to dig up the Ximen canal embankment, making it impossible to protect the city of Youcheng. The general residents were all greatly alarmed, and the society became unstable. Fearing that these farmers might actually commit such illegal acts, Magistrate Wang ordered the military police to go to the Ximen, the sluice gates along the river, and the head sluice gates to defend them, and the people's hearts were slightly settled. Today, the Junhe water level is still rising as before. The Yu Wharf water level has reached one zhang and nine chi. It is said that the dam water arrived in Xinghua this afternoon. The second, third, sixth, eighth, and ninth districts of the county have been completely flooded, and the autumn harvest is hopeless. Because a famine is emerging, the rice mills in the city have seen the price of rice skyrocket by sixty cents per dan, and there is still a tendency to rise further. The county has suffered successive famines in recent years, and now it has been hit by this flood, which is truly unfortunate for the people of Youcheng.

Simplified Diagram of Various Dams Draining into the Sea 90

Jiangdu

A dispatch from Gaoyou on the 6th states that at 6:00 PM yesterday (4th), there was a sudden downpour, accompanied by a strong northwest wind. The Grand Canal's water level suddenly rose from one zhang and nine chi to one zhang, nine chi, and six cun. The waves, driven by the wind, directly washed against the embankment, which was extremely dangerous. All the teachers and staff of the education sector, as well as the employees of various shops and agencies, wore straw sandals and carried high poles and lanterns to work on the embankment. Fortunately, by 8:00 PM, the rain had stopped and the sky had cleared, but the wind was even stronger than before. The new additional sub-embankment at the Miaohangkou and Hehuatang outside the North Gate had collapsed by several feet due to the impact of the huge waves. They immediately sounded the gong to rush to the rescue. After receiving the report, Magistrate Wang immediately ordered Shen Qi, the first platoon leader of the police team, to lead his team to open the new dam together with the Water Conservancy Bureau, and personally rushed to Miaohangkou and Hehuatang to direct the rescue efforts, and the situation was resolved. Unexpectedly, at that time, a new additional sub-embankment on the Ximen Canal embankment suddenly collapsed by several zhang and was extremely dangerous. Suddenly, gongs sounded inside and outside the city, and the people were terrified. Many people climbed onto the city walls to take refuge. Magistrate Wang rushed to Ximen again to supervise the embankment protection work. Before Ximen had escaped the danger, reports of overflowing water came from the Yu Wharf, Tonghu Bridge, and Huayan Temple one after another. Fortunately, there were many workers, and the situation was resolved through emergency repairs. Only at 1:00 AM this morning did the northwest wind stop, and the canal embankment was no longer in danger. The citizens of the entire city did not get a good night's sleep. Residents outside the city, during the extremely dangerous times, all flocked to the city to take refuge. Today, the water level of the canal embankment, due to the cessation of the wind, the Yu Wharf water level has dropped to one zhang, nine chi, and three cun. It is now learned that the Nanguan Dam was also secretly opened last night. Magistrate Wang has ordered the accumulation of soldiers at the four city gates this morning to block the north and south water gates in preparation for closing the four city gates in the event of an extremely dangerous situation to prevent accidents, and refugee shelters have been established in the city. It has been determined that the public education center, Qianming Temple, Yaowang Temple, and other 40 locations will be used as the shelter sites. At around 10:00 AM this morning, a gong sounded again, reporting that the moat near the city had broken and the head sluice gate was leaking. Upon hearing the alarm, the general residents were greatly alarmed. Each family was busy building water pavilions, because if these two locations were to fail, the water would flood into the city. Fortunately, after emergency repairs, there are no problems. Currently, the three dams in You territory have been opened. If the canal water continues to rise, the people of the entire city of You will likely be buried in the bellies of fish. (August 5th)

A dispatch from Zhenjiang states that since the Cheluo Dam was opened on the 2nd, the water level of the canal in Jiangsu province has continued to rise. On the 3rd, the Yu Wharf rose by one cun, with a water level of one zhang, eight chi, and nine cun. Mao Yisheng, the director of the Provincial Water Conservancy Bureau, and the resident engineers sent by the various departments of the provincial government,

Page 10

telegraphed the provincial government from Gaoyou to report the increase in the water level, saying that it was not enough to relieve the crisis without continuing to open the Nan (Nanguan Dam) and Xin (New Dam) dams. Director Mao returned to the provincial government on the 4th to attend the provincial government meeting and reported everything. It was decided that if the water level continued to rise and was deemed critical, the Nan and Xin dams would be allowed to continue to be opened. It was reported to the Water Conservancy Bureau that the Yu Wharf water level had increased by one cun each on the 4th and 5th, with a water level of one zhang, nine chi, and one cun. Therefore, the Xin Dam, which drains into the sea, was opened again yesterday. The Nanguan Dam has already overflowed, and it will inevitably be opened within days. As for Yaowan Yishui, it suddenly surged by one meter and fifteen centimeters on the 4th, with a water level of nineteen meters and twenty-six centimeters. The Huai River in Bengbu fell by five centimeters, with a water level of nineteen meters and eighty-six centimeters.

A dispatch from Yangzhou states that the canal's water level was initially expected to gradually decrease after the Cheluo Dam was opened. Unexpectedly, in the past three days, the water flow along the canal has still been increasing. As of the 5th, the Gaoyou Yu Wharf water level had risen by two cun again, with a total water level of one zhang, nine chi, and one cun. Therefore, the New Dam was opened again yesterday, and the Nanguan Dam also overflowed, and it will inevitably be opened within days. However, after these two dams are opened, whether the disaster in the counties of the Lixia River will not worsen is a major question. Furthermore, although the dams continue to be opened, if the water continues to rise, it will inevitably lead to breaches. Therefore, the provincial government and the Pacification Supervisory Office view protecting the embankments and rescuing them as the only task amidst the calls to open the dams. It was recently heard that the Jiangdu County Government received a telegram from the provincial government, relayed by the Water Conservancy Bureau, stating that the canal embankments should be protected by the various construction offices, which should convene civilians to protect them in order to avoid breaches. After receiving the telegram, the county government immediately ordered Section Chief Lu Shiquan of the Second Section to go to Shaobo Town to supervise and manage the matter and protect the people's fields. Furthermore, Zhang Zhijiang, the Pacification Supervisor, believed that the matter required the joint efforts of the military and the administrative aspects due to the severe flooding, and yesterday issued a general order that the troops stationed along the canal should unanimously maintain the river embankment. As for how to handle the matter, they should contact Section Chief Qian and Director Mao of the Water Conservancy Bureau, who were sent by the provincial government, at any time for proper consultation. (6th)

Hangzhou Express Mail 92

The Zhejiang province is issuing public bonds to reorganize old debts, with a fixed amount of eight million yuan. The provincial government has resolved that various government agencies and county governments should allocate and solicit funds. The Director of Finance, Wang Zhengying, regarding these public bonds, plans to establish a foundation management committee and the issue of deposit at a certain bank. He took the night train to Shanghai yesterday to negotiate with the banking sector.

The provincial government, based on a report from the Taiwan compatriots' association in Hangzhou, has repeatedly received letters from compatriots in various counties reporting continuous heavy rains and rice crops being submerged. Villages near the mountains in Ninghai, Tiantai, and Xianju counties have also suffered from mountain torrents. It is requested to forward the appeal to urgently order various counties in Taiwan to suspend the issuance of rice export permits and allocate funds for disaster relief to save the affected people. Yesterday, the Zhejiang Relief Committee and the Civil Affairs Department were ordered to investigate and handle the matter.

The Construction Department believes that the silkworm industry in Zhejiang province is deeply and significantly related to the social economy. The administrative meeting of the Construction Department has resolved to implement measures to improve the silkworm industry and has ordered all cities and counties to investigate and implement them.

In the agricultural fields of Jin, Qu, Wen, Tai, and Chu, many early rice crops have been planted and are now reaching maturity and ready for harvest. According to reports, the recent continuous rain has not affected them, and a good harvest is expected. The time for offering new rice will be in late June. (6th)

Local Communications

Songjiang 93

Two Bandits Executed: The issue of the bandit suppression commander of Songjiang, Jinshan, Jiashan, and Pinghu counties. Two bandits, Shen Shanlai and Chen Xingsheng, who were previously identified as committing robberies in Zhangyan, Ganxiang, and other places, were sentenced to death in accordance with the Regulations for the Punishment of Bandits. After receiving approval from superiors, Commander Cao, upon receiving orders, identified Shen and Chen on the morning of the 6th, verified their identities, and escorted them to the execution ground at Yuhuang Pavilion for execution by shooting.

Donating Houses to Benefit Students: The houses in the Du Gong Ancestral Hall in the city have been dilapidated for many years. As they are connected to the school buildings of the Songjiang Middle School under the province, the First District Office donated the land of the ancestral hall. At the same time, the school established six free admission quotas for students recommended by the First District to show gratitude and benefit poor students. After repeated consultations between the two parties, and approval from the relevant higher authorities, representatives were appointed to sign a contract and transfer the ancestral hall's land on the 6th.

Education Association Rescues Education from Stagnation: The County Education Association held a temporary membership meeting yesterday (the 5th), and Shen Fuyun was publicly elected as chairman to discuss the issue of how the association should try to rescue the situation to avoid educational stagnation, as it was reported that the teaching staff of primary and secondary schools in the county have decided that if the budget for the 20th year is not satisfactorily resolved by the start of the school term, they will postpone the start of school. It was resolved to send telegrams to relevant agencies in the province and county to seek urgent relief. Furthermore, regarding the issue of whether the association should appropriately subsidize the maintenance expenses of the district education associations, which were established in April of the 19th year, from the beginning of the 20th year, it was decided to subsidize each district education association with ten yuan.

Suzhou 94

Robbery Case at the Rice Experiment Field to be Solved Within a Deadline: The Jiangsu Provincial Rice Experiment Field, located in Huguan Town, Suzhou, was suddenly attacked by five or six bandits dressed in gray military uniforms and armed with firearms the day before yesterday. They arbitrarily searched and robbed the field, stealing more than 500 yuan in cash. The Public Security Bureau is paying close attention to this case and has ordered its subordinates to solve the case within seven days.

Another Wave of Disputes Arises at Xuanmiao Temple: The dispute over demolishing the screen wall of Xuanmiao Temple to rebuild houses has lasted for more than a year. After the Public Security and Construction Bureaus forcibly demolished the bowl shops of the Xiang and Jiang families last month, construction of houses has begun. However, the Construction Bureau has not complied with the directive from the Executive Yuan to move the original screen wall in for reconstruction. The general preservationist faction believes that the Director of the Construction Bureau has violated orders and neglected duties, and they are very dissatisfied. As for the demolished bowl shop owners, they also believe that the Construction Bureau has violated laws and colluded to exert pressure. After appealing to the Hubei Compatriots Association in Shanghai, the association sent four people, including Wang Bu and Cheng, to Suzhou yesterday (the 6th) to petition the county government, demanding the removal and punishment of the Director of the Construction Bureau.

Anti-Japanese Movement Registers Japanese Goods: The Wuxian Anti-Japanese Aid Overseas Chinese Association is starting with the registration of Japanese goods to carry out the boycott of Japanese goods. The deadline is set for the 14th, and registration forms have already been distributed to various industries with a deadline for filling them out. The Wuxian Chamber of Commerce's Committee for Economic Severance with Japan held its second meeting yesterday (the 6th). (1) It was resolved that the registration of Japanese goods would be free of charge. (2) The Cloth Factory Association requested that the difficulty of Japanese yarn be noted and forwarded to the Anti-Japanese Aid Overseas Chinese Associations in all circles for record-keeping. It was resolved to comply.

Education Workers Oppose Budget Cuts: The education funds for urban and rural areas of Wuxian County for the whole year amount to more than 620,000 yuan. This time, the Education Bureau, under the instructions of the Education Department, is implementing budget cuts, reducing the total budget by about 10%. As a result, people in the education sector are extremely alarmed upon receiving this news. The Education Association convened a general meeting of the entire body yesterday morning (the 6th). It was unanimously resolved on the spot to organize a temporary executive committee, elect 21 committee members, and petition the Education Department to maintain the original state of the 19th year.

Jiangyin 95

Reasons for Police Detectives Arresting the District Head: On the night of the 31st of last month, Fang Guozhen, a secret agent from the county police team, and Liu Wenjin, an informant, led the arrest of Sun Jinxi, Sun Sanguan, Wang Goulang, and Yin Xiaojianzi, the perpetrators of the robbery case at the home of Huang Guangen in Lanmen Sha in the spring of the 17th year of the Republic. At that time, Chen Xipei, a neighbor, opened the door to investigate because Wang Goulang's wife was calling for help. Fang Guozhen and others called him a communist, beat him with ropes, and dragged him to Wang Guangen's house for private interrogation. After Ding Jinshu, Gu Changyuan, and others intervened, he was released after paying 20 yuan, with 10 yuan paid now and the remaining to be paid in three days. Chen, suffering this injustice, went to the Third District Office to petition the District Head, Xu Kuizheng, to investigate. Xu then sent militiamen to arrest the perpetrators, but Fang Guozhen and others had already fled. He also questioned Wang Goulang and others, who all stated that Fang Guozhen had extorted money in the dark. Later, they were sent to the Houcheng Third Sub-Bureau. Fang Guozhen went to the county to report that Chen Xipei had extorted money and released the perpetrators, feigning injury for verification, and obtained Order No. 2 from the county. On the 3rd, he brought seven policemen from the Wangjiadai Police Team to the District Office to demand the release of the people. Xu claimed that the group had been sent to the Houcheng Third Sub-Bureau. Fang went to the Third Sub-Bureau, asking them to hand over the people. Director Zhang of the Sub-Bureau replied that since the bandits were sent by the Third District Office, they should still be sent to the Third District Office, and there was no reason for him to hand them over. Fang then went to the District Office again. District Head Xu stated that since there was no private seal of the trial officer on the warrant, he could not release the people. Fang became furious and, together with the seven policemen, arrested District Head Xu and escorted him to the city. The township heads of the district believed that the District Head was the leader of the entire district and was arrested and humiliated by Fang Guozhen. This not only lacked legal basis but also caused a loss of face for the entire district. They held a meeting yesterday (the 4th) and unanimously agreed to rescue him, demanding that the county government dismiss Fang Guozhen and punish him severely. They appointed Zhong Yanxin, Sun Xueshan, and others as representatives to petition the county. In the afternoon, District Head Xu personally presented the case to County Magistrate Peng, demanding strict handling according to the law. This afternoon, after summoning Chen Xipei, Wang Goulang, Fang Guozhen, and others for questioning, further action will be taken.

Court Interrogation of Conflict Between Militia Police and the Big Sword Society: Zhang Guangde, a small shop owner of Yongji Noodle Shop in Houcheng, Second District, and a member of the business militia, was taken away by the Big Sword Society (local defense group) of Zhuxiang, Zhouzhuang. This was because Zhang was implicated by Gu Zigen, who claimed that he had participated in the robbery case at the home of Sha Tingxiang. The Houcheng Business Militia and the Third Sub-Bureau of Public Security went to search, resulting in a conflict. At the same time, Zhou Jigen was killed, and Xu Bingxiang and Ding Zuomei were drowned. All eight people arrested on both sides, including Hou Youwang, Li Yaoting, Sun Chufa, Zhang Guangde, Gu Zigen, Zhu Kunru, Zhu Jinyan, and Song Shanlang, were interrogated by Trial Officer Wu on the afternoon of the 3rd. Each person's testimony differed. Zhang Guangde and others arrested by the Zhouzhuang side denied being bandits, and Hou Youwang and others newly arrested by Houcheng denied being members of the Big Sword Society. As a result, all were released on bail pending further questioning.

Nantong 96

Conflict Between Smuggling Suppression Soldiers and the Security Corps Resolved Through Mediation: A conflict occurred between the soldiers of the Yangba Salt Smuggling Suppression Camp stationed in the Fourth District and the Yiyu Security Corps. On the 5th, County Magistrate Zhang Dong, Salt Affairs Inspection Office Commissioner Zhou Pan, and Smuggling Suppression Camp representative Shi Zhuocheng mediated at the county government, releasing the four salt soldiers arrested and handed over to the county. Both sides returned the seized weapons and ammunition, and the misunderstanding was resolved.

Business Tax Collected Quarterly: The Nantong Business Tax Bureau, upon the order of the Department of Finance, has determined the recognized amount of business tax in the city. It should be collected quarterly at 8,000 yuan. Director Jin Yanhai has requested the Chamber of Commerce to summon various industries to quickly pay the recognized amount. The tax will be levied from April 1st. The request to the province to extend the deadline by three months was not approved.

Disaster Relief Through Labor in the Eastern Townships: The eastern townships of the county have been severely affected by floods. The county government convened a post-disaster meeting and formulated measures to provide relief with a combination of short and long-term approaches. A committee has been established to dredge the Huanghai, Anwang, and other ports and is implementing relief through labor.

Wuxi 97

Successive Reports of Famine: Zhao Hongbin, the head of the Seventh District (Huai Shangshi), reported that Chen Songxian, the head of Datongqiao Township, stated that the Wu family embankment in Wu Lane of the township, with two areas of varying sizes totaling 278 mu, and about 660 mu in Sutang Township, have been submerged three times. The planted seedlings have all rotted, and the future harvest is likely hopeless. Furthermore, Lin Xizhen, the head of the Eighth District (Huai Xiasheng), reported that Shao Yuanfa, the head of the Xiqi Township, stated that about 10,000 mu of fields in the township have been flooded. After receiving the reports, Zhao and Du, the two district heads, submitted a written report to the county government yesterday, requesting that officials be sent to conduct on-site inspections, exempt from historical taxes, and provide immediate relief.

Rape of a Young Girl Referred to the Court for Trial: Zhou Guilin's daughter, Zhendi, a resident of No. 8 Damage on Houqili, outside the North Gate of the city, who is only six years old, was raped by Zhu Ayuan, a neighboring cook. As a result, Zhendi's lower body was covered in blood and severely swollen. After Guilin and his wife learned about it, they immediately handed Ayuan over to the Fifth Branch of the Public Security Bureau, which transferred him to the General Bureau. Yesterday, Director Xu of the Public Security Bureau submitted a written report to the County Court. After Chief Zhou opened the court for preliminary interrogation, he ordered the coroner Shen Zuchan to examine Zhou Zhendi's lower body in detail. It was found that there was white secretion inside, but the rape could not be proven. Zhou ordered Zhu Ayuan to be detained, and Zhou Guilin and Zhou Zhendi were ordered to return home, pending further investigation by the Prosecutor's Office after Zhendi was sent to Puren Hospital for diagnosis.

Thorough Investigation into Accumulated Financial Funds for Dyke Repair: During the 14th year of the Republic, Hu Yixiu, the former director of Tianshang Township in the Fifth District of the county, withdrew 800 yuan from the funds for dyke repair and stored it in Wang Yuanji Smeltery as funds for dyke repair. Over the years, the interest accumulated to more than 400 yuan. However, due to changes in municipal administration, these funds have been repeatedly transferred. Recently, due to sudden floods, the dykes in the entire district are about to breach. Farmers have petitioned the District Office to allocate these funds for dyke construction. However, after investigation, only 200 yuan remained. The remaining principal and interest were all embezzled by the former District Head, Hu Zhongfang. The district residents, Fan, and others, have jointly organized local public groups to conduct a thorough investigation and have petitioned the county government for a thorough investigation and strict punishment.

The Owner of a Foreign Goods Store Suddenly Disappears: Sun Jinghong, the owner of Wanxing Foreign Goods Store in Shitangwan Town, Wananshi, the Sixteenth District of the county, brought funds to the city on the 2nd to purchase goods. He had said that he would return that night, but he has been missing for five consecutive days. His wife, Tang, is panicked and unable to sleep or eat. She has entrusted friends to search in various parts of the city and countryside, but there is still no news. The mystery remains unsolved.

A Dissolute Youth Commits Suicide by Jumping Off a Train: There is an Yifeng Tobacco and Paper Store next door to the Zhongnan Grand Theater on Xinmin Road, Yingshan River Estuary, in the city, which is opened by Zhou Xiangqi. His son, Huimin, who is 19 years old and likes to wander around, suddenly disappeared five days ago. After searching for him without success, Zhou Xiangqi suddenly received a fast letter sent from Xiaguan, Nanjing, the day before yesterday. When he opened it, he realized that it was sent by his son Huimin. The letter stated that he needed 500 yuan and asked to send it to Beijing quickly, otherwise, he would commit suicide. While Zhou was frowning in distress after receiving the letter, Huimin had already returned to Wuxi by train from Beijing. When the train was traveling to Yangqi outside the North Pengkou, Huimin suddenly jumped off the train, causing serious injuries. A policeman who saw this immediately sent him to the sanatorium for treatment.

Changzhou 98

Results of the Re-election of Provincial Representatives: The representatives elected in the preliminary election of Wujin for the Second Provincial Representative Assembly held a re-election meeting at the County Party Headquarters on the 5th. The Provincial Party Headquarters specially sent Chen Fugang to Changzhou to supervise the election. Thirty-two representatives from the preliminary election attended. As a result of the election, Gao Bozhen, Xue Digong, Zhuang Minqiu, and Sun Youguang were elected as representatives to the Provincial Representative Assembly.

Partner Flees with Money, Clues Discovered: Xi Zhenxiang, a partner of Yongfengsheng Timber Company outside the West Gate of Wuyi, recently took a Zhuang account book to pay more than 8,400 yuan at various villages and then fled without a trace. After the company sent people to investigate, they learned that Xi Zhenxiang had become acquainted with a woman surnamed in Sunfu Alley in the city in May. This time, he fled with the woman and is likely to have fled to the Suzhou-Shanghai area. The company has sent people to various places on the 5th to investigate.

Danyang 99

Organization of Water Disaster Relief Committee: Danyang has suffered a second flood, unseen for more than a decade. The county government has frequently telegraphed the province for relief and has organized a Water Disaster Relief Committee to take charge of the situation. A meeting was held yesterday, and the following were immediately appointed as members: the County Government, the County Party Headquarters, the Public Security Bureau, the Finance Bureau, the Construction Bureau, the Education Bureau, the Agricultural Improvement Field, the District Offices, the Property Office, the County Farmers' Association, the County Police Team, the Farmers' Bank, the Grain Management Committee, the Cooperative Guidance Office, the Grain Association, the Silk Industry Association, and gentry members such as Jiang Kesheng, Yin Moqing, Lin Lishan, and He Gengyun. The committee was established immediately.

Bandit Attempts to Escape by Jumping into River: Jiang Shuyou's house in Jiangxiang Township in the eastern region was robbed by bandits. The Public Security Bureau's investigation team captured four bandits, including Jing Lailai, and handed them over to the county for preliminary interrogation. According to their confession, a fellow accomplice, Zhou Binghai, had participated in the robbery of Zhang Hesheng's house in Qiganxia and burned the victim, sharing the loot. It was also stated that Zhou was hiding in Nanduan Village. The team leader, Huang Qi, led police detectives to arrest him. The bandit Zhou attempted to escape, but fortunately, the police officers were lying in ambush outside the door. When they saw the bandit Zhou escaping, they stepped forward to arrest him. In desperation, the bandit jumped into the river but was eventually captured. He has now been handed over to the bureau for interrogation.

Zhenjiang 100

Two Bureau Chiefs in Liyang Accused of Embezzlement: The Jiangsu Provincial Construction and Education Departments previously received reports from the people of Liyang accusing Shi Ziquan, the Director of the Construction Bureau, and Zhu Yufeng, the Director of the Education Bureau, of embezzlement and malpractice, harming the people in violation of the law, and requesting their removal from office and investigation. They have all been informed to the newly appointed County Magistrate Chen of Liyang to investigate and handle the matter impartially. It is now heard that evidence has been found and reported to the provincial departments for strict handling according to the law.

Yangzhou 101

Collecting Wages on Behalf and Strangling to Death and Burial: According to a report from the rural guard Xu Longqing to the Tenth Branch of the Public Security Bureau, Guo Linchen and Mao Lintian Longjiang of Hongzhuang, Yugaqiao, beat Guo Dawanzi severely, strangled him with a rope, and buried him in a nearby desolate tomb, with a peach tree stake nailed around it. On the evening of the 1st, Patrol Officer Rao Qilu was dispatched to lead the police to investigate and arrest the suspects Guo Linchen and Xia, the wife of Longjiang, to the bureau. It was stated without denial that the victim was accidentally injured during an altercation while collecting half a yuan in unpaid wages on behalf of Chen Xiaocaizi. The suspects then buried the body. After obtaining a guarantee from the rural guard to watch over the body, the suspects and the rural guard have been handed over to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation and then transferred to the County Court. Yesterday (the 3rd), the prosecutor of the court, Ju Dongchen, went to the village for examination.

Welcoming and Bringing the Bandit Leader for Trial in Yangzhou: The Pacification Superintendent's Office received a complaint from Zhang Delu and others that Dong Zhengren (Dong Shouer), a bandit leader in Jurong, Zhenjiang, had fled to Shanghai. He has already been handed over to the British Concession Police in Shanghai and transferred to the Special Zone Court. They also stated the facts of the victim and requested that they be welcomed and brought back for trial. Special permission was granted to send a team to welcome and bring him back. He has now been brought back to Yangzhou. After Director Xu of the Military Law Court confirmed the facts, he instructed the plaintiff to return temporarily, and Dong Zhiren will be detained pending trial.

Pinghu 102

Filial Piety Kills His Own Father: Lu Deyuan, a tailor in Dongshengtang Village, is relatively wealthy. His son, Along, is as fierce as an owl. The night before last, Along asked his father for money but was refused. In a fit of anger, he immediately restrained his father, Deyuan, and punched him. His mother tried to persuade him in vain. Deyuan had a pre-existing condition, and as a result of this attack, he died immediately. Seeing that he had committed a major disaster, Along ran away. Lu's wife then reported to the county, requesting verification of the cause of death, arrest of the murderer, and severe punishment.

Bandit Zhang Jinkui Sentenced to Imprisonment: The bandit suspect Zhang Jinkui gathered a group of people to rob the farmer Shen Quanhe's house with weapons last year. He was arrested and sent to the county government, and then detained for a long time. Now, Shen Quanhe's uncles and nephews submitted a written report to the county for questioning, proving that Zhang was indeed the perpetrator. Yesterday, Song, the trial officer of the county government, sentenced Zhang to one year and two months of imprisonment in court. The number of days of detention before the decision will be deducted from the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day. He was sent to prison to report the execution.

Hangzhou 103

All Sections of the Hangzhou-Changxing Highway are Fully Open: After passenger cars resumed operation on the Hangzhou-Changxing Highway, only a dozen miles of the road surface from Yangjiabu to Changxing were still submerged by floodwaters, reaching a depth of six or seven feet, causing a partial interruption of traffic. Recently, after several sunny days, the water level gradually receded. The Provincial Highway Administration, recognizing the importance of traffic, tried to pump water. As of yesterday, the water level on the road surface was only a little over a foot, and fortunately, the road surface was not damaged. Vehicles have resumed operation today. The wooden stakes planted by villagers on the Liangzhu section have been completely removed after persuasion. All sections of the entire road are now open as usual.

Guangde 104

Communist Party Horrifyingly Murders the District Head: Shawan, Guangde, is located in a remote mountainous area. In recent years, the Communist bandits have been entrenched and extremely rampant. Although the garrison troops have been dispatched to suppress them, it is still difficult to completely eradicate them due to the thick mountains and forests. On the 2nd of this month, the newly appointed District Head Yang of the Fifth District of the county went from the city to take office. The escorting military police consisted of about 60 people. On the way, they were suddenly surrounded by a large number of Communist bandits when passing through Banbiantian. Banbiantian is a notoriously dangerous mountain valley, with narrow sheep trails that can only accommodate one person at a time. On the left is a steep mountain, and on the right is a small river. At that time, the military police were outnumbered, and the terrain was cramped, so after a fierce battle for 20 minutes, they retreated with cover from box cannons. It is estimated that four officers and soldiers were killed on the spot. The new District Head Yang was captured and horribly murdered. Four quick-firing guns, 200 bullets, and 800 yuan in military pay were lost. It is also heard that the Tobacco and Alcohol Bureau also lost some tax revenue, and the tax collector Chen suffered minor injuries.

Hefei 105

Chairman Chen Returns to the Festival from Lu'an via Hefei: Chen Diaoyuan, the Chairman of the Anhui Provincial Government, inspected the area around Lu'an, Huoshan, and Sujiabu, overseeing the suppression of the Red Bandits, achieving successive victories. On the 21st, he returned to Lu'an from Huoshan. Due to repeated telegrams from the Central Government calling him to participate in the bandit suppression conference, he arranged the military affairs and left Lu'an on the 26th by sedan chair. He stayed overnight at Guanting Town, on the border of Hefei and Lu'an. On the afternoon of the following day, he arrived in Hefei around 4:00 PM and stayed at the military headquarters. Various public groups prepared a banquet to welcome him and presented the tragic situation of the two floods, requesting exemption from this year's land tax. Chairman Chen agreed to order the Finance Department to handle it. At 10:00 PM, he left Hefei by steamboat. Military, government, police, and various public groups bid farewell as usual.

Aftermath of the Second Flood: Hefei has been in a state of misery since the second flood on the 25th and 26th. Many people have been left homeless. The Red Cross has specially set up shelters to provide porridge and meals, reaching over a thousand people in a single day. However, the flood victims in the northwest city are blaming Zheng Yaotang, who is responsible for the Shuixi Gate dam, for handling the situation poorly. Furthermore, they are blaming the Gu Lou Bridge circle, which has been blocked by business firms, and the Jiu Shi Bridge circle, which has been occupied by poor people, for causing the unrest. On the afternoon of the 27th, people from all walks of life held a meeting at the First Public Office to discuss and resolve the matter. They presented a report to the county requesting that Zheng be dealt with, either by fining him 400 yuan or by parading him through the streets with a cangue. They requested that the County Government Construction Bureau send workers to dredge the Gu Lou and Jiu Shi Bridge circles and raise funds to repair the city's rivers. They also appointed dozens of people to form a water disaster relief and temporary river dredging committee.

Letter

Letter from the Hushu Pass Dayou Silkworm Seed Manufacturing Plant 106

Respectfully, I read in your newspaper's August 4th local communications column, under the Wuxi section, that Qingcheng City, Qianzhou, Yuqi, Beiqi, and other places have ordered a total of 360,000 tiger-branded silkworm seeds from the Dayou Seed Manufacturing Plant. Currently, various merchants, knowing that the mulberry trees are submerged in water and the mulberry leaves are withered, believe that it is not suitable for the silkworms to eat them, so they have no intention of raising them and have been returning them to the seed manufacturing plant. This is absolutely not true. The information reported in your newspaper must be based on false rumors. Please disclose this letter to clarify the situation and avoid misunderstandings. Respectfully, Hushu Pass Dayou Silkworm Seed Manufacturing Plant, 8.5.

Letter from the Nanhui County Party Department Rectification Committee 107

Recently, I read a news item in the local communications column of your newspaper on August 5th regarding the "election dispute of provincial and national representatives" in Nanhui. It does not conform to the facts. On the 2nd, the county held a re-election meeting for representatives to the Provincial Representative Assembly. Prior to the meeting, the department sent employees to different district branches, and those that qualified as a representative were selected by the law. There were 35 representatives. That day nineteen showed up, and the Provincial Rectification Committee sent the fifth-district instructor, Li Songjiao, to supervise. Around 2:00 pm, Zhu Baozhong and other five representatives asked to meet with the supervisors and left, delayed until 3:20. The supervisor, seeing the statutory number of representatives, and having surpassed the stated deadline, announced the meeting would begin. So-called refusal of representation, the department informed attendants of that fact. How could they be rejected afterwards? There is no reason or fact for this at all. Especially the mention of heavy weaponry and an intense environment, it's completely unheard of. That day, six police officers were dispatched to maintain order. It is feared that confusion would be spread. I ask that you place the original message in the incoming message section to illuminate the truth. Nanhui County Party Department Rectification Committee, August 6th.
