Hunan Education Circles Petition for the Completion of Independent Education Funding 110

Changsha Dispatch: The education circles of Hunan have been tirelessly advocating for the independence of education funding for several years. Although the Executive Yuan approved a surcharge of two yuan and three jiao per package of foreign salt, only eight jiao per package was actually received, amounting to just over 90,000 yuan per month. The monthly education budget for Hunan requires 300,000 yuan. If the full amount were allocated (over 260,000 yuan per month), it could barely be sustained. However, the current shortfall is significant, making it difficult to maintain. Therefore, after deliberation by representatives of various schools, in addition to sending Fang Kegang, Hu Yuantan, and other representatives to explain the situation to the central government, a formal petition was submitted to the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Finance, and the Ministry of Education, based on the Provisional Constitution, requesting the direct allocation of funds from the salt tax or customs duties to achieve independence. The text of the petition to the Executive Yuan is recorded below:

Petition for the Implementation of the Central Government's Previously Approved Independent Education Funding, in Accordance with the Provisional Constitution, to Safeguard and Maintain Education: It is noted that Hunan Province's education funding was once allocated eight jiao from the salt tax surcharge and managed independently, which proved convenient for many years. Subsequently, due to the gradual development of education, with annual needs exceeding three million yuan, the originally allocated eight jiao per package proved to be significantly insufficient. Education circles therefore submitted a petition to the government in the spring of the 18th year of the Republic, requesting the allocation of one yuan and five jiao from the salt tax surcharge in Hunan, totaling over 260,000 yuan per month, to achieve the independence of education funding. This was approved by the Executive Yuan in May of that year, reported to the National Government for record, and the Ministry of Finance was instructed to transfer the allocation, while the Ministry of Education notified the Hunan Education Department for information. In May of the 19th year, the Hunan Special Finance Commissioner was instructed by the Ministry of Finance to allocate additional funds. Subsequently, upon reading reports that the salt tax surcharge had a limited term and was to be collected by the Ministry of Finance, academic circles expressed concern that Hunan's education funding was fundamentally threatened. They detailed the special difficulties in Hunan Province and petitioned the Executive Yuan to maintain the established case and complete independence, and appointed Hu Yuantan, Lei Zhuohuan, and eight others to go to Beijing to fight for it. Unexpectedly, last year, the Ministry of Finance unified the salt tax, still calculating based on the old amount of eight jiao, resulting in only 93,100 yuan per month being allocated by the Hunan Salt Transportation Bureau. Consequently, Hunan Province's education funding suffered a monthly deficit of 174,000 yuan. It is considered that Hunan has been plagued by banditry and natural disasters for many years, and its financial constraints are even more severe than before. Various schools are struggling to survive due to limited funding, while the public's knowledge is gradually increasing, leading to a growing number of applicants to schools. However, schools are unable to accommodate them all, leaving young people wandering aimlessly, which is a major hidden danger for the country. Furthermore, during the period of political tutelage, education is a fundamental construction. The late Premier Sun Yat-sen clearly stated in his political program the need to increase education funding. This year's Provisional Constitution of the Republic of China for the Period of Political Tutelage, Article 53 of Chapter 5, also clearly stipulates that the central and local governments should generously allocate necessary funding for education and ensure the security of lawfully independent funding. Currently, the salt tax surcharge of two yuan and three jiao per package, which was approved by the central government for allocation to Hunan Province, is indeed lawfully independent funding. The established case is clear and can be reviewed. Hunan is suffering from the aftermath of chaos, with impoverished people and depleted resources. Even if the central government does not generously allocate education funding, the one yuan and five jiao of this lawfully independent education funding of two yuan and three jiao should be protected by the Provisional Constitution and implemented. Kegang and others, in order to comply with the Provisional Constitution and complete the independence of Hunan Province's education funding, respectfully petition your Excellency with three requests: (1) The previously approved additional allocation of one yuan and five jiao from the salt tax surcharge, totaling 174,000 yuan per month, is requested to be implemented from the Hunan salt tax surcharge and directly transferred to the Hunan Provincial Education Funding Management Committee for safekeeping, in accordance with the established case. (2) Alternatively, please approve the allocation of 174,000 yuan per month from the Changsha Customs duties as Hunan Province's education funding, and instruct Changsha Customs to comply and directly issue the funds nearby. (3) If not allocated from Changsha Customs duties, then please directly allocate 174,000 yuan per month from the central government as Hunan Province's education funding, to be transferred to the Hunan Provincial Education Funding Management Committee for safekeeping. These requests are made only because of special difficulties, and we would not dare to repeatedly implore. However, the Provisional Constitution is a creed to be observed by all, and the independence of the above-mentioned education funding is an established case approved by the central government. Based on facts and legal principles, these are not excessive demands. We earnestly request your Excellency's prompt consideration and clear implementation, so that Hunan Province's lawfully independent education funding can have a reliable guarantee. We are at the point of anxiously awaiting orders, and we respectfully submit this petition.

Anhui Education Department Organizes Provincial School Properties 111

Apart from a portion of the school properties under the Anhui Education Department being houses in Anqing City, the remainder are river islands. Lai Zi Island in Huaining County belongs to the Provincial Education Association and is currently temporarily managed by the department. Da Sha Tu in Fanchang County, Ba Du Lake in Dongliu County, and Chongwen Island and Tieban Island in Tongcheng County are all directly under the jurisdiction of the department. In view of the complex conditions of these river islands and the frequent changes in land, it is impossible to verify the actual number of acres. The rents and taxes collected in the past, due to the customary practice of assigning personnel to collect taxes according to acreage, only totaled over 10,000 yuan per year, making it difficult to achieve substantial improvements. It is necessary to immediately conduct a land survey and organize these properties to increase the revenue from school properties. The department has submitted a proposal to the provincial government meeting, requesting instructions on the methods for organizing provincial school properties. It has also drafted a simplified charter for the Provincial School Properties Organization Committee. The proposed committee members, in addition to the heads of the Civil Affairs, Finance, Construction, and Education Departments as ex officio members, will also include several members appointed by the provincial government. The head of the Education Department will concurrently serve as the chairman of the committee. The committee will have three sections: organization, collection, and affairs, responsible for all matters related to their respective sections. This charter has been discussed and approved by the department's affairs meeting and will be implemented upon approval by the provincial government meeting.

Songjiang

Middle and Primary School Teachers Fight for Education Funding 113

| Held Second General Assembly... Vowing Not to Start School Until Goals are Achieved

Since the new standards for Songjiang County's education funding were established in the 17th year of the Republic, they have been barely maintained. Subsequently, due to repeated provincial orders to reduce the living expenses of education personnel, the situation has been deteriorating daily, yet they still struggled to support it. However, after provincial investigator Xu Xihuang arrived in Songjiang to conduct an investigation, he disregarded the facts and falsely reported to the Education Department, resulting in the arbitrary reduction of Songjiang's education funding, making it impossible for teachers and staff to maintain their livelihoods. Forced by these circumstances, they united all the teachers and staff of the county to fight for their rights. Yesterday afternoon at 1:00 PM, the third general assembly was held in the auditorium of the People's Education Center, with over 300 teachers and staff from middle and primary schools attending. Xu Rensen chaired the meeting, and Tang Zhenzhi served as the secretary. After the formal proceedings, the chairman gave a report, followed by a discussion of the proposals. (1) If a satisfactory solution to the budget for the 20th year of the Republic has not been reached by the time school starts, in addition to each school announcing a temporary postponement of school, should a declaration be printed and posters pasted to inform all sectors of society of the truth? It was resolved to pass this proposal and appoint Mr. Song Renwei and Mr. Chen Guisanyi to draft the declaration, which will be submitted for approval at the next general assembly and then published in major newspapers in Shanghai. (2) Chongming County's education funding has also been arbitrarily reduced by the Education Department. How should this association express its support in a letter requesting assistance? It was resolved that the Education Department's austerity policies affect more than just Songjiang and Chongming counties, and a telegram should be sent to urge the education associations of various counties to organize a provincial education association to take the lead in fighting for their rights to maintain local education. 3. The Education Department's reduction in funding is destroying education. Request that the county's representatives attending the provincial assembly present this issue for discussion and assistance at the assembly. It was resolved to pass this proposal. 4. In the case of the Education Department's reduction in funding, the primary schools have not yet received official documents. An investigation has revealed that they have been shelved by the education committees of each district. Should this association make a statement? It was resolved that this association should send a letter to the education committees of each district, sternly questioning them. The date for the next meeting was set for 1:00 PM on August 12th. The meeting was then adjourned.

Free Talk

World Snippets 137

— Seafarer

Strange and Terrifying Plants

Dr. Killip of the Smithsonian Institute led a group of scientists to collect plant specimens in the upper reaches of the Amazon River and the mountains of Peru in South America. Despite hardships and setbacks, they achieved remarkable success. In February of last year, they returned to Washington, bringing back no less than thirty thousand species of strange and diverse plants. Some could kill, some could induce bizarre dreams, and some could paralyze fish while leaving their meat edible. Among them were thousands of species previously unknown and unnamed. For example, one type of vine called Ayahuasca, also known as Caapi, is used by native apothecaries to create drugs. When ingested, these drugs cause drastic reactions in the nervous system. Another plant produces a milky sap with anesthetic properties. Native people pour this sap into rivers when fishing, quickly paralyzing the fish across a large area of the river, rendering them helpless. Fishermen then easily capture them one by one. Strangely, the poison does not affect the fish’s meat, which remains edible after cooking and has no unusual taste. The name of this plant, however, remains unknown.

Two Righteous Men on Dongmen Island 138

— Carefree

Sanmen Bay is located in the center of the national coastline, serving as the gateway to eastern Zhejiang. The land is fertile, and the produce is abundant. Opposite Shipu Town lies Dongmen Island, which is recorded in the Book of Han as Tianmen Mountain. The terrain is extremely dangerous. During the Tang Dynasty, Changguo Garrison was built on the island's summit to guard against pirates. The island is surrounded by water, with raging waves. In foggy or hazy weather, the port becomes indistinguishable even at close range, making it a feared passage for ships. The Tiger Reef, which faces the island, is particularly treacherous. Careless navigation can lead to disaster. Yesterday, I traveled to Sanmen Bay on business and took the opportunity to visit the lighthouse on Dongmen Island. The tower was built by two fishermen brothers, Ren Xiaohe and Xiaofu. It stands over thirty feet tall and houses a kerosene lamp that is lit at night, shining like a solitary star in the darkness, guiding navigators and ensuring safe passage.

The Ren brothers, who make a living by fishing, used their life savings of several thousand gold coins to build the lighthouse. They also constructed two houses next to the tower, with four rooms in the front and three in the back, to provide rest for travelers. The furnishings are elegant, and the walls are adorned with couplets written by Yu Zhishao, Zhang Yishan, Ma Gong, Yu Yutian, and Sui Zengnong, all praising them as righteous men. After building the tower, the Ren brothers' wealth was depleted, and they lived a simple life with coarse clothes and poor food, which is truly commendable. Their deep concern for the benefit of society shames the hoarders of wealth.

When I met the righteous man Xiaohe, he was dressed in a short garment of coarse white cotton cloth, barefooted, with hair hanging down to his shoulders, and a face tanned dark brown, indicating a long history of weathering storms. Yet, his passionate and deep emotions were revealed in his smiles and conversation. The lighthouse requires over seven hundred gold coins annually for oil and other maintenance costs, which they have never sought from outside donations. Instead, they rely on their daily fish sales to cover the expenses. Someone once suggested to the authorities that the lighthouse be taken over by the province to ensure its permanent operation. However, this only resulted in the province claiming insufficient funds and rejecting the proposal. Thus, Ren and his brother continue to brave the waves, endure the wind and rain, and diligently fish to maintain the oil expenses.

After our meeting, the righteous man Ren cordially offered me a meal, featuring delicious aquatic dishes with unique flavors. He also led me to the top of the lighthouse, where I could gaze into the distance, taking in the beautiful scenery of the water and mountains. The sea breeze howled, and my sleeves fluttered, making me feel as if the autumn god had descended to earth. Who would have known that it was the scorching heat of the dog days of summer? After several hours of tea and conversation, I was treated to handmade cakes of lichen and millet flour, which were delicious and unforgettable. Alas, he spends private wealth for public benefit, avoids worldly disputes, and relies on his own efforts. Compared to those who strive for power, profit, fame, and reputation, his virtue is vastly different. I recall the couplet given by Mr. Yu: "Two righteous men in the mountains, the first lighthouse overseas," which is truly fitting. I lingered for half a day and wrote a few words before departing, as a memento. The text reads: "In July of the twentieth year of the Republic of China, I traveled to Sanmen Bay, passing through Shipu and visiting the Tianmen Mountain lighthouse. I was warmly received by the righteous man Ren Xiaohe. After spending half of his life diligently laboring and finding joy in fishing, he spends private wealth to benefit the public and guides the world with a beacon of light. The spirit of benevolence and harmony should be as immortal as this tower. I had heard of him for several years and finally met him today, enjoying the beautiful scenery and the peace of half a day. I am immensely pleased and wrote these words to leave a trace and express my gratitude."

Man Jiang Hong 139

— Xiangheng

Fine rain enshrouds sorrow, aimlessly stirring, spring colors fill the garden, curtains half-drawn. Begonias spread like embroidery, evening mist solidifies green. A parrot startles awake from a dream of fragrant grass, embroidered stationery wears out by a scholar of blue skies. But the courtyard at dusk is quietly empty, crows return urgently. No more to be said, a flute before the wind. Love and hate, still like weaving. Sigh, silken thread, helpless to bind spring. Lonely painted boat on the jade pond, hesitating swallows speaking under carved beams. Facing a cold ten-mile expanse of apricot blossoms on the flat lake, who pities them?

Wuji Boxing 140

— Silent

The art of combat in our country originates from the practices of nurturing life. The bear-walking, bird-stretching, and five-animal exercises of the life-nurturing schools are derived from the ancient people's leisure activities of music and dance. The transformation of music and dance into life-nurturing practices connects with Taoism. Thus, music and dance represent the whole, while the animal exercises and external strengthening represent parts, each with its own emphasis. During the Five Dynasties period, Bodhidharma resided at Mount Song. Shaolin Temple has a tradition of Bodhidharma's exercises. Later, several of his disciples assisted Emperor Taizong of Tang in defeating Wang Shichong, earning titles. Emperor Taizu of Song once taught his skills to the Shaolin monks, hence the Shaolin tradition of Taizu Boxing. Yue Wu Mu was framed by Qin Hui, and his skills were acquired by the Shaolin monks, thus the Shaolin tradition of Yue Family Hand. Consequently, Shaolin became a general repository of combat techniques. During the Yuan Dynasty, Grandmaster Zhang Sanfeng became acquainted with the Shaolin monks, exchanging Taoist arts with them. After mastering their essence, he modified them into a soft boxing style. He also dreamt of the Xuan Emperor imparting boxing techniques. Later, he secluded himself in Wudang Mountain, leading to the distinction between the Wudang and Shaolin schools. Grandmaster Sanfeng, proficient in elixir studies and versed in the principles of the Book of Changes, created three sets of grand boxing techniques, Wuji, Taiji, and Bagua, each consisting of one hundred and twenty-eight moves (totaling three hundred and eighty-four moves to match the three hundred and eighty-four lines of the Book of Changes). These were secretly treasured by eccentric individuals and passed down privately, resulting in fragmentation and incompleteness. It is not easy to gather even fragments to form a whole. However, those who have obtained the genuine transmission of the three sets of techniques in one breath have maintained a single line of transmission that has never been severed. Mr. Zhou Tianxiang studied under Mr. Peng Zufan of Xuzhou in his youth and obtained the genuine transmission, combining the strengths of both the Wudang and Shaolin schools. He once traveled to Han Gao and now comes to Shanghai. Those who have long admired him gathered fellow enthusiasts and invited Mr. Zhou to demonstrate his skills at Qingliang Temple in the Xin Family Garden. On the second day of the national calendar, Mr. Zhou generously attended the gathering and performed all one hundred and twenty-eight moves of the Wuji Boxing. The exquisiteness of his techniques, the agility of his movements, the solemnity of his expression, and the completeness of his energy circulation were such that only one who had truly grasped the essence of soft boxing could achieve such excellence. Those present at the demonstration included Wu Huichuan, Ye Dami, Ji Rongwu, Jiang Zhuzhuang, Jingbo the old monk, Lü Zibin and his son, Huang Xingruo and his son, a certain lady, and many other guests. After watching the performance, all applauded and praised him. All knowledge in our country originates from the teachings of the Book of Changes. Although much has been lost and scattered, if one can diligently seek, one can find treasures of the past sages everywhere. Boxing is one such example. If Mr. Zhou can make public the three sets of life-nurturing grand boxing techniques and the famous boxing techniques of the Shaolin school in the future, they will not only be suitable for the old and the young, the civil and the martial, prolong life, and prevent illness, but also indirectly release unique splendor from ancient music, dance, and the images of the Book of Changes, strengthening the country and the race, and promoting the ancestors. All of this depends on him. Therefore, I take up my pen to record this. (No payment accepted.)

Stealing Half a Day for a Trip 141

— Master Embracing Qin

I have long admired the beauty of Tiger Hill, but I have never been able to visit due to being overwhelmed with worldly affairs. A few days ago, the Tianyi Film Company went to Suzhou to film exterior scenes for "Spring Colors on the Singing Stage." Mr. Shao invited me to accompany him, and I took the opportunity to visit Tiger Hill. A wish that had been cherished for years was finally fulfilled, how delightful! The ancients said, "Stealing half a day of leisure from busy life." Now I can say that I have "stolen half a day for a trip from busy life."

That morning, I took a car from the company to the North Station. Soon, the staff and actors also arrived one after another. After getting on the car, laughter and chatter filled the air. Xuan Jinglin was especially witty and amusing. When the car arrived in Suzhou, we got off and immediately filmed exterior scenes of the train station. Zhang Yongcui played a flower seller, wandering on the platform with a flower basket. Those who did not know the truth mistook her for real and even tried to buy flowers from her. After filming at the train station, we took a horse-drawn carriage to the Garden Hotel and filmed another three or five shots before having lunch. By then, it was 1:30 PM. Everyone was very hungry. As soon as the food arrived, spoons and chopsticks flew, and the dishes were quickly emptied, like clouds swept away by the wind. After lunch, everyone returned to Shanghai, while I hired a car to go to the Xuanmiao Temple. When I arrived, I was greatly disappointed, as there was nothing to see except for the stalls. After walking around once, I visited my old classmate, Mr. Wang Shenxuan. Mr. Wang is a famous doctor in Suzhou. We had been separated for almost ten years, and we were very happy to see each other. He accompanied me to visit Tiger Hill. On the way, the mud was everywhere, and the wheels of the car got stuck in the mud and could not move forward. The two coachmen had to push and pull the car to move forward. When we arrived at the gate of Tiger Hill Temple, we got out of the car and walked. Mr. Wang led me around to see almost all the scenic spots, including the Sword Pool and the Thousand-Man Rock, which I had seen in the film "Tang Bohu." It was like revisiting an old place. We went to the Cold Fragrance Pavilion to have tea. The layout of this pavilion is very similar to the Misty Rain Tower in Jiaxing. It is surrounded by plum trees. If it were winter, the faint fragrance and sparse shadows would be even more interesting. Because I was anxious to return to Shanghai, I took a quick look and took a car directly to the train station. On the way, we passed through Shantang Street, where the flood had submerged the banks, half a foot deep. The coachman waded through the water, as if the car was driving on water. This reminded me of when I read Mencius, who thought it was almost humorous to say that Zichan used his carriage to help people cross the Zhen and Wei rivers. I didn't expect to experience it myself today. After arriving at the station, I bought a ticket and boarded the train. The whistle blew, and the wheels turned. Looking out the window, I could still see the North Temple Pagoda standing tall in the hazy twilight.

Travelogue of India (76) 142

— Linghua

On the 7th, after contacting people from both Indian and Islamic religions, I then observed their society. From my observations of India, I have reached some understanding. Moreover, upon looking at historical records, I have come to realize the reason why the Indian and Islamic peoples cannot cooperate lies in the fact that they will never cooperate on religion. Indian society is vegetarian, reveres gods, and seeks liberation in life. It is like the teachings of immortals and Buddhas going back to the time of Chao Fu and Xu You and even earlier. Islam uses courage and force to establish countries, with religion as the foundation. It is meat-eating, reveres Heaven, is strong and roams in Central Asia, seeking to conquer and subdue dissenters. There is a saying that scholars cannot reason with soldiers. This describes India and Islam. Looking at the entire history of India, the Macedonians entered and ruled it, as well as the Greeks, the Mongolians, the Muslims, Persians, and Afghans, and more recently, the British. Indian religion does not discuss politics, which lacks political thought, thus allowing other forces to exploit the gaps. This is India. Our China takes the middle way as the teaching, but lacks philosophy and religion. Buddhism entered and dominated, and also lacks material sciences, thus allowing material sciences to enter and dominate. Each nation has their own specialized strengths and characteristics, helping and complementing each other. In the future, I hope our country deeply delves into the material sciences and further develop our middle-way politics and principles of people's livelihood. By taking advantage of the gaps in Europe and making up for its shortcomings, we will create great unity, and who can do this but the Chinese? Alas, looking at the frequent wars in India, it is clear that pure sages, immortals, and Buddhas are not enough to govern. When Greece fell, Roman barbarians plundered its philosophers, celebrities, and beautiful women, turning them into slaves of savage peoples. Thus, Greek philosophy is not enough to govern a country. Looking at the rampage of Napoleon and the ferocity of Genghis Khan, which disappeared without a trace, brute force alone is not enough to govern a country. Our China has eight words: managing heaven and earth, civil and martial achievements, sages and heroes, yin and yang, rigidity and flexibility, complete and without deficiency. This is why China is China. As for the religious issue, the 20th century is no longer a major problem, but the Indians and Muslims are still obsessed with it, which is not what we are eager for. China is concerned with the issues of people's livelihood and human life.

That day, there was a Buddhist monk named Shamin Shenxin, Satyacleo (transliterated as Shitetui), an Indian follower who had just returned from the United States, passing through Europe before returning to India. He was about fifty years old and wore a light yellow robe. He gave a lecture in the auditorium. I unfortunately did not understand Sanskrit and did not know what he was saying. However, thousands of students applauded continuously for about a minute. I admire the way Indian students applaud, with rhythmic cadences like music. Two thousand people applauding is like a large organ. This is a characteristic of Indian students. The monk Shamin Shitetui told me that the wishes of the Americans for Asia, India, and China are only to sell goods and make money. However, there are now many followers of Indian religion, and there are Indian churches in major ports. I regret that China has no religion to transmit abroad, and no one is transmitting Buddhism to foreign countries, leaving us in a position to receive teachings from others.

Rotary Club of Novels

Women Women (12) 143

— Yao Sufeng

Mr. Lu was getting jealous. He had originally envied Miss Ding, but for the past few months, despite his wasted efforts, writing many letters and making many phone calls, he had not received a comparatively optimistic response. However, he had not felt hopeless. He still believed that Miss Ding had a good impression of him, so he continued to pursue her passionately.

Now, he actually saw Miss Ding come to play with Little Lu, and he heard Little Lu say that he had invited her. Remembering that he himself had invited her to play golf three days ago, and she had not agreed, he felt like he had been struck three serious blows.

There were no other conversations at the time. Miss Ding smiled at Mr. Li and continued forward with Mr. Lu. The more Mr. Li looked, the angrier he became, and the more he thought, the more furious he became. He realized that he had already been defeated by Little Lu.

Finally, after all eighteen holes were played, Mr. Lu calculated the recorded scores. Miss Ding's score was better, with a total of sixty-four strokes, while Mr. Lu himself had seventy-three strokes.

"The term 'golf' is truly wonderful. Naturally, I should let you have the upper hand," Mr. Lu laughed heartily.

"Why should you let me?" Miss Ding still didn't understand the meaning of these words.

"If you interpret the three words 'golf,' doesn't it mean 'surpass your husband'?" He laughed even louder.

Miss Ding was not angry at all, only feeling a bit shy. But in her entire mind, it was clearly a most precious memory and an extremely stimulating pleasure.

They chatted and laughed, everything immersed in the dissolving scenery. Only Mr. Li, who was constantly peeking over there, felt it was a great humiliation and had to leave disappointedly and resentfully.

Although Miss Ding grew up in Shanghai, she felt some disgust for the bustling urban life. She wanted to travel to a place with beautiful mountains and rivers during this vacation. Now she felt she could have this opportunity.

"I'm tired of playing in Shanghai. I want to go to Suzhou for a few days. You're from Suzhou, you have to fulfill your duties as a host!" Miss Ding said with a smile.

Mr. Lu felt somewhat uneasy when he heard that Miss Ding wanted to go to Suzhou. He thought of the Suzhou train station and felt it posed a great danger to him. He had to say indirectly, "I think Suzhou is not as good as Hangzhou. Besides Hangzhou, Taihu Lake in Wuxi is also really good."

"No! I've already been to Hangzhou several times, and I don't want to go to Wuxi. I think it's better to go to Suzhou. It's convenient to go and return, and besides, it's your hometown!" Miss Ding seemed to express herself very firmly.

Gold Price Rebounds Rapidly 145

Small fall, big rebound… up seven taels eight mace

Triggered by the sharp drop in the British pound. Yesterday, the gold price trended upward again. The progression was good, and the fluctuations were moderate. However, there were over eight taels of fluctuations from morning to night. In the end, the price rose by eight taels, reversing the previous days' losses of just over seven taels. This is a sign of a slow retreat followed by a swift advance. The price rose from the opening, likely due to the slight increase in the silver market. The sharp drop in the British pound internationally, Germany's plan to buy cash from the United States, and the declining US stock market boosted confidence. Major players actively bought, and the North Bank's cash outflow was significant. The market became increasingly bullish, exceeding 740 taels. The foreign exchange market was also tight. In the after-market, the situation was very stable, fluctuating by only one tael. Transactions were not as active as in the morning. The exchange rate stabilized, with the final price at around 44 taels. This morning, the large bars show a trend of falling, but the gold market is not expected to weaken. However, there may still be some sideways movement.

Progressive rise after the opening. The opening price for September was up 1 tael 2 mace at 737 taels 2 mace. The price of silver rose by one-sixteenth of a tael, and the telegraphic rate rose by one-eighth of a tael. The private telegraph rate rose by only one-sixteenth of a tael, so it was not significant. Then, due to strong buying interest from Cuichangyong, Dadecheng, and Zhifengyong, the price rose from 36 taels 8 mace to 39 taels 8 mace. It then fell slightly by one tael to 38 taels 6 mace, due to sales by Wanxing, Tongtaichang, Shunli, and Yuancheng. The first order was issued without change, and Dongyang added 0.25, then increased to 39 taels 5 mace. As for the trend in silver prices, based on the situation last month, there was initially an upward trend. Currently, due to the unresolved anti-Japanese sentiment, the demand for silver has not had an opportunity to surge, so it remains sluggish.

Dormant Demand for Silver Dollars 150

The sluggish demand for silver dollars this year is unprecedented compared to last year. The large-scale spring and early summer silkworm cocoon season was fleeting. Subsequently, the demand for summer cocoons was even more stagnant. For nearly two months, the demand for silver dollars from out-of-town customers completely disappeared. As a result, the silver dollar price trended downward, with no hope of rising. According to news from spot traders, the Yangtze River basin is experiencing a severe shortage of silver dollars due to the recent floods. Therefore, starting yesterday, there has been a rush to purchase from the Shanghai market. However, the quantity is limited and not for formal use. It is estimated that the demand is only for 1-2 million. Yesterday and the day before, shipments to various locations totaled 3-400,000 each. Demand from other areas remains stagnant. It is expected that there may be an opportunity for strong demand after the autumn cools down. Therefore, the current silver dollar price may see a slight improvement.

Yarn and Cotton 152

Sudden Sharp Drop in the Yarn Market 153

External Markets Continue to Decline...Actual Sales Stagnant

Long Positions Cut Losses Painfully...Market Prices Plunge Straight Down

The long-brewing yarn market suddenly experienced a sharp drop, with the situation being very weak. The overseas cotton yarn situation is trending downwards, with no end in sight. Additionally, widespread flooding is impacting actual sales, and trade on all routes is stagnant. Sichuan yarn prices plummeted by 10 taels, and Guangdong yarn prices also fell by 3-4 yuan. Numerous negative news items arrived in quick succession, leading to significant wavering among long positions. Scattered long positions had to endure painful liquidations, resulting in a straight plunge in market prices. However, given the treacherous trends in the global cotton market, further price declines are still possible. Some believe that prices may even fall to around 50 taels.

Human Labels Fall by 2.7 Taels: Trading on the exchange for human labels opened lower in the morning market due to negative news and falling U.S. cotton prices. Prices fell by 1.3, 1.4, and 1.5 cents across various months, with the second and third rounds of trading remaining weak. As a result, prices fell by 1.48, 1.49, and up to 2.3 cents. The afternoon situation remained weak, with each month falling by 0.4, 0.6, 0.7, 0.8, and 0.9 cents. The total volume traded was 52,750 bales. Sold: Yiyu 1,750 bales, Jifeng 2,400 bales, Shenyu 1,650 bales, Lichang 3,000 bales, Tianlong 1,150 bales. Bought: Daji 1,900 bales, Gongtai 2,750 bales, Tongyu 4,100 bales, Senkang 1,300 bales, Yuantai 1,350 bales, Yichang 1,250 bales. The closing prices for human labels are recorded below:

Spot Yarn Also Falls by Over 2 Taels: Sales of spot yarn are exceptionally quiet. A total of 250 bales were purchased by various domestic dealers throughout the day. Internal dealers purchased 300 bales. Prices fell by over 2 taels. Domestic dealers imported 75 bales from the interior, 25 bales from Tianjin, 25 bales from Qingdao, and 30 bales from Sichuan. Miscellaneous dealers imported 35 bales.

Violent Decline in the Cotton Market 154

Treacherous Global Trends

Foreign Merchants Compete with Price Cuts

The cotton market is very weak, and the sharp decline has been brewing for some time. However, the majority of people in this city are holding firm due to the severity of the flooding. Recently, the prices of Indian and American cotton have fallen sharply, making silver-based calculations cheaper. Therefore, domestic cotton is struggling to stabilize. However, the situation in the American cotton market is extremely pessimistic, and foreign merchants, seeing the urgency of the situation, have been forced to cut losses. The market is becoming increasingly weak, and there are reports of foreign cotton being sold off at reduced prices. Each factory is hesitant to take action due to the deteriorating environment. Some say that Japanese factories have already purchased 30,000 dan of Lumite cotton at 39 taels, and the spot goods are being delivered to the factories.

Han Labels Fall by 0.95 Cents: Trading on the exchange for Han labels opened lower in the morning market due to a sharp drop in Indian cotton and weak American cotton. Selling pressure was strong, with prices falling by 0.055 to 0.08 cents across various months. The afternoon situation remained weak, with prices falling by 0.015 to 0.03 cents. The total volume traded was 146,300 dan. Sold: Taixing 5,000 dan, Xincheng 2,000 dan, Xinfeng 2,300 dan, Heshen 2,600 dan, Yichang 2,700 dan, Beiji 3,700 dan, Yuda 1,500 dan. Bought: Tongyu 2,200 dan, Yicheng 2,200 dan, Xinheng 2,000 dan, Yichang 2,700 dan, Gongtai 2,700 dan, Houfeng 2,700 dan. The closing prices for Han labels are recorded below:

Spot Sales Completely Stalled: Spot cotton trading is becoming increasingly quiet. The trend of foreign cotton is becoming more treacherous by the day, and each factory is taking a wait-and-see approach. The source is estimated to be 1,400 bales of Yao cotton.

Foreign Yarn and Cotton Continuously Trend Downward 155

U.S. Cotton Spot Sells at 8 Cents: Yesterday, U.S. cotton was weak due to unfavorable news from Liverpool and good harvests. Sellers pressed prices down. Futures fell by 0.16 to 0.19 pounds, and spot fell by 0.15 pounds. British cotton futures fell by 0.09 to 0.10 points, and spot fell by 0.14 points. Egyptian cotton spot fell by 0.25 points. The Indian cotton market was weak, with Pingguoer and Aomula falling by 4.75 rupees and Bailuoxi falling by 7 rupees. The original telegram is recorded below: (August 5th telegram)

Grains: Smooth Sales in the Hexia Rice Market 156

South Market: There was a slight supply of various types of rice from Hexia yesterday, with limited inventory. The market rebounded due to the gradual increase in foreign rice prices and the firmness of the North Market. Dealers showed some buying interest, and the price of thick japonica rice suddenly increased by 0.2-0.3 cents. There was not much early indica rice arriving, and although the demand from Ningbo was weak, the local sales were still active, leading to another increase of 0.02 cents. The arrival of Luyang Jianyuan foreign rice is increasing daily, with strong demand and a rising trend. The sales of Yinhua rice are good when available, and the trend is stable. The supply of foreign rice remains tight, with activity from the Han dealers and some local purchases. Prices are gradually firming. Over 100 shi of Dongxin japonica rice arrived yesterday, stabilizing the price at 14.5 yuan.

New Zha: The supply from the West Road is slightly less, and the market is not smooth. There is a lack of early indica rice arrivals, and the bulk price suddenly increased by 0.4-0.5 cents. People are watching closely. The prices of Su Chang Machine Japonica rice and Kunshan rice have each increased by 0.2 cents. Although there is some South Port early rice on the docks, the quantity is not large, and the price has also increased by about 0.01 cent. The sales of Lubu Jianyuan rice are sluggish, with no change in price. Wine shops and food vendors purchased nearly 1,000 shi of glutinous rice, and the price increased slightly by 0.02 cents. The Hexia factories have a volume of 6-7,000 shi.

Flour: Continuing Imports by Out-of-Town Dealers 157

Yesterday, the flour market showed an initial state of stability. With a slight decrease in the price of foreign wheat by 0.02-0.04 cents, sentiment among industry participants was naturally depressed. Although the opening price for this month reached 3.2105 yuan, the floods in the country, both north and south, have caused unprecedented and unparalleled devastation. Therefore, dealers from various regions are still purchasing actively. Impartially speaking, given the situation in the country, the current market value seems reasonable. However, with the continued dumping from foreign countries, it seems that the shorts are intending to make adjustments. As a result, the current month remained unchanged, September increased by 0.005 yuan, October and November increased by 0.0025 yuan, and December increased by 0.005 yuan. January was up 0.0025 yuan.

Wheat Market: Recovery After Weakness 158

Yesterday, the wheat futures market showed signs of weakness, with the price for the current month reaching a low of 4 taels, but it soon recovered. Trading in the distant months was relatively sparse, and the market was stable. By the afternoon opening, the longs for the current month were unwilling to move lightly, and given the significant floods and expected food losses, buyers remained firm. As a result, the current month was unchanged, September increased by 0.01 yuan, October and November increased by 0.02 yuan, and December increased by 0.01 yuan. The spot wheat market remains stable. Over 5,000 bags of Wusong, Xu Gongqiao, Shuangfeng, Zhitang, Wuxi, Yangzhou, and Luzhu wheat were opened and handled by Huafeng and Fuxin.

Silk and Tea: New York Silk Market Has Prices but No Sales 159

Factory Silk Remains Expensive with No Demand

New York has historically been the largest consumer of Chinese silk. In recent years, due to economic instability in various countries and the declining sales of silk fabrics, silk weaving factories have increasingly focused on rayon to reduce costs. Furthermore, Japanese silk has taken the opportunity to compete with low prices, causing the American sales of Chinese silk to suffer a setback. Shanghai white factory silk has not seen any transactions since March of this year. Recently, some silk factories have occasionally made supplemental purchases of futures to prepare for production, but they still find Shanghai factory silk too expensive and there is no demand. The demand for gray raw silk and Sichuan and Shandong yellow factory silk is also stagnant, with prices but no sales. However, trading in Japanese silk futures and spot is quite lively. It is reported that over 1,000 bales have been sold this month.

Grey Raw Silk Prices Remain Weak in American Sales 160

Yesterday, the Shanghai foreign silk market continued to be quiet. Although overseas silk factories are gradually becoming more active in purchasing futures silk, there are still no positive reports on Chinese silk. Grey raw silk prices remain weak in American sales. Yesterday, only Dachang made a supplemental purchase of 20 bales of high-grade grey raw silk to cover shortages, and Samsung purchased 10 bales of white raw silk. The price remains stable.

Core-Picked Zhenmei Tea Skyrockets by Over 10 Taels 161

Yesterday, major firms such as Jinlong, Yihe, Xiehe, and Yongxing were highly interested in core-picked Zhenmei tea from Wuyuan and Tunxi. The top price for high-grade Wuyuan goods opened at 240 taels, and the market price skyrocketed by over 10 taels. The shrimp-eye pearl tea market was more active than before. The sales of needle-tip tea and phoenix-tip tea were also firm. Although there was no major development in the Gongxi market, white-top dealers, anticipating the upcoming Russian season, also had a tendency to search for purchases.

North-South Goods: Slight Improvement in Dried Lily Flowers 162

Since the new crop of dried lily flowers came to market this year, the various firms have had different goals, and the company has failed to form. Therefore, each firm has been acting independently, and market prices have frequently fallen, resulting in significant losses. As a result, sales in various regions have also been sluggish. The various firms, fearing a repeat of this situation, are planning to reorganize the company and unite to work together to maintain market prices. This is expected to be realized, and the market price has already shown a slight improvement. If sales improve in the future, the opportunity for recovery will be just around the corner.

Sugar Market: Both Taikoo and Market Sugar Turn Upward 163

Yesterday, according to news from sugar-producing areas, the price of Cuban spot sugar was unchanged, while New York sugar futures fell by 0.01 to 0.03 cents. Both Javanese spot and futures showed little fluctuation. In the Public Association market, the price of Dutch sugar #24 coarse white sugar was stable, but both sales and purchases were slack, and trading was scarce. The asking price remained at 11.3 taels, while Hong Kong goods were at 11.2 taels. The price of #20 medium white sugar was at 10.085 taels, and the market was still firm. The price of Cuban red sugar increased to 9.95 taels, as it is used by ice sugar factories to produce ice-flower sugar, and demand is quite strong, making the market very firm. Trading in Taikoo cane sugar was quite active. B was at 11.09-11.0925 taels, CW was at 11.0725-11.075 taels, DY was at 11.07 taels, HX was at 11.07 taels, and HM was at 11.02 taels. The market was firm and brisk. The Public Association has several hundred bags of ice-flower green sugar offered at 10.035 taels. The market is brisk, and there are no signs of further price increases.

Hardware: Arrivals Are Strong but Sales Are Stagnant 164

Market Overview: Yesterday, the hardware market continued to be quiet. Both retail and wholesale trade with out-of-town dealers were minimal. Although factories made some transactions, most were just for adding assorted goods. As for staple goods, there was still no good demand. Unfortunately, arrivals continued unabated, leading to a situation of full inventory and reduced sales. The overall market situation was somewhat sluggish. However, with recent exchange rate stability and positive sentiment, there was no panic in the market, so this can be stated with certainty.

Frequent Arrivals of Imported Goods: In the past two to three days, the number of hardware imports has been very large. Therefore, warehouses such as New Taikoo, Gonghexiang, and Zhaoshang Zhongbei, as well as piers such as Dalai and Osaka, are all facing problems of being full. Among them, the inventory of scrap iron is the most abundant. Among the new goods, English 10-gauge plates, tinplate, flat white iron, and new lead wire are also quite popular. However, 8-gauge 26-foot black iron sheets are still not arriving, so prices have been able to remain stable without falling.

Export Business Is Stagnant and Inactive: The hardware export business to various ports has been stagnant and inactive recently. Although sales are usually sluggish during the summer season, this year is worse than ever. The reason is that various regions have been affected by flooding, and Shi Yousan's betrayal has severely impacted business in Tianjin. As a result, the hardware market trend feels very deserted.

Local News

Jiang Zuobin Appointed as Envoy to Japan 187

Shigemitsu Officially Appointed as Minister to China

Jiang's European Trip May Be Cancelled

Wang Rongbao Went to Beijing Yesterday Morning

The Minister to Japan, Wang Rongbao, accompanied by his staff member Ren Jiafeng, went to Beijing by special express train at 9:30 yesterday morning to meet with the Minister of Foreign Affairs, Wang Zhengting, to report on the results of the investigation of the Korean case. Wang has been appointed as the Director of the Asian Department of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. The National Government has decided to appoint Jiang Zuobin as the Minister to Japan. The Japanese government officially expressed its agreement yesterday. Before Jiang takes office, the secretary of the embassy in Japan, Jiang Hongjie, will act as the agent. It is reported that Jiang was summoned to Jiangxi by Chairman Jiang's telegram to discuss this matter. At the same time, according to news from the Japanese Consulate, the Japanese government officially appointed the Acting Minister Shigemitsu Kui as the Minister to China yesterday, and immediately formally notified the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. The relationship between China and Japan should have new developments. Jiang Zuobin and Shigemitsu Kui made the following remarks to Chinese and Japanese reporters yesterday.

Jiang Zuobin's Remarks: A reporter from the Far East News Agency specially visited Jiang at his private residence at 5:00 PM yesterday and asked whether he had received a formal order for the change of his appointment as the Minister to Japan, and whether his attendance at the League of Nations meeting would be cancelled as a result, and whether he would go to Japan to take office first. According to Jiang, he originally planned to take the Fengtian Maru from Shanghai to Dalian on the 9th of this month, and then go to Russia to attend the League of Nations meeting in Europe. His luggage had just been packed when he suddenly received news of his change of appointment as the Minister to Japan. However, he has not yet received a formal order, so he is not in a position to express any opinion to you. However, if this matter is true, his attendance at the League of Nations meeting may be cancelled, and he cannot predict it. In short, everything will be done in accordance with the orders of the National Government.

Shigemitsu's Remarks: Shigemitsu Kui, the newly appointed Japanese Minister to China, told a group of Japanese newspaper reporters yesterday that he was deeply frightened by the new order he received today (that is, yesterday). But in reality, his duties have not changed in any way. The only difference is the name. In the future, he will continue to work hard to promote the development of relations between China and Japan.

Emergency Disaster Relief Association for Flooded Provinces

Grand Inaugural Meeting Held Yesterday 188

Telegraphic Request to the Government for Prompt Allocation of 20 Million in Cash

Organize 500 Fundraising Groups, Each with 1,000 Yuan

The Shanghai Emergency Disaster Relief Association for Flooded Provinces held its inaugural meeting at the City Chamber of Commerce yesterday. More than 200 people attended, including Xu Shiying, Wang Yiting, Yu Qiaqing, Wang Xiaolai, Ha Shaofu, Wang Peiyuan, Qin Runqing, Zhang Zhijiang, and Wang Yansong. Xu Shiying, Wang Yiting, and Wang Xiaolai were publicly elected as the presidium. After Yu Qiaqing reported the purpose of the meeting, Wang Xiaolai and Wang Yiting spoke successively, detailing the severity of the floods in various provinces and the urgent need for relief. Subsequently, Xu Shiying reported on the flood situation in 16 provinces including Anhui, Hunan, Jiangxi, Henan, Jiangsu, Hubei, Fujian, Zhejiang, Hebei, and Guangdong. In general, he said that the continuous rain and mountain floods had caused deaths and displacement, which was an unprecedented catastrophe in nearly a hundred years. He asked for urgent fundraising to provide relief. As a result, Wang Xiaolai proposed two solutions: (1) In the name of the meeting, telegraphically request the government to promptly allocate 20 million in cash for relief; (2) Organize fundraising groups to raise funds separately, with 1,000 yuan per group, and set up 500 groups. Regardless of whether they have arrived today or not, those who have been invited by letter will all be executive members of this association, and they are requested to designate at least one group, and it is best to recognize several groups. The entire venue unanimously approved. Those who signed up on the spot accounted for 75,400 yuan. Others who have not yet committed will be sent to contact them. The rest of the proceedings will be discussed at the next committee meeting. The meeting adjourned at nine o'clock.

Yesterday's News on Expanding the Concession 189

Merchants in Western Shanghai Have Begun to Deny

The Western newspapers fabricated the story that merchants in Western Shanghai had requested the Municipal Council to expand the concession. Legitimate merchants in that area have now begun to deny this. The truth of the matter will soon be revealed. The following is a continuation of what we have heard:

Denial by Merchants and Residents of Zhoujiaqiao: Gu Hongjun, Chen Zhenbo, Lv Xuehai, Ji Jinwen, Zhu Fangjie, Yuan Lianghong, Jiang Qinsheng, Bao Benchu, Zhang Yongqing, Lu Shirong, Hong Liangqing, and other merchants and residents of Zhoujiaqiao in Western Shanghai, saw a news report in a major American newspaper that 200,000 merchants and residents of Zhoujiaqiao, Wangjialou, and Shengjiaqiao in Western Shanghai had jointly requested the Municipal Council to expand the concession. They all believe that the merchants and residents of Western Shanghai are not all ignorant people. How could they have such a heartless and crazy idea of ​​flattering foreigners and willingly acting as accomplices? Even if there are one or two local ruffians who are willing to be lackeys of the Municipal Council, their despicable behavior is only their own private opinion, and how can they pretend to be representatives of 200,000 people in Western Shanghai? They do not know what basis the Municipal Council relied on, or what methods it used, to obtain the so-called joint request of 200,000 people in Western Shanghai, and even published a propaganda-style record in a major American newspaper. Is this kind of trick using ronin to impersonate public opinion? Once an investigation is conducted, the truth will come out. But the merchants and residents of Western Shanghai, for no reason, bear this evil reputation of flattering foreigners, inviting people to spit and scold them. How can they remain silent? Therefore, yesterday, they convened people from all walks of life and held a special emergency meeting at the Zhoujiaqiao Security Corps. They all said that the contents of the newspapers and the letters requesting the Municipal Council to expand the concession were absolutely denied by the citizens of Western Shanghai, and they submitted a document to the party and government authorities requesting a strict investigation of the heartless and crazy representatives who impersonated the request, and requested them to forward it to the Municipal Council to find out the source of the letter of request in the name of others, in order to emphasize sovereignty and extend genuine public opinion.

Statement by the Municipal Committee of the Pusong District: The Guomin News Agency said that after the news of the merchants in Western Shanghai requesting the expansion of the concession was published, the reporter of the Guomin News Agency specially visited Chen Yafu, a member of the Municipal Committee of the Pusong District, for the sake of clarifying the facts. According to him, he was extremely shocked after reading the news in the "Great American Evening Post" that merchants from Chenjiaqiao, Zhoujiaqiao, Wangjialou and other places in Western Shanghai had jointly requested the Municipal Council to expand the concession. He secretly said that he has always been the most vocal advocate for the recovery of the concession and the recovery of roads built beyond the boundary. The merchants in the newspaper's publication are located within the scope of the Pusong District, and he has an inescapable responsibility. Therefore, he went to Wangjialou Zhoujiaqiao (that is, the Zhu Jiaqiao in the newspaper's error) and Chenjiaqiao (that is, the Sheng Jiaqiao in the newspaper's error) and other shops yesterday in the sweltering heat to conduct a detailed investigation. They all said that at this time of singing loudly about the recovery of the concession, no sane merchant would dare to do such a wicked thing and do something against his conscience. They absolutely deny the sections published in the "Great American Evening Post." The merchants in the towns and villages in the Pusong District of Western Shanghai are all well-informed and enthusiastically participate in every patriotic movement. The groundless rumors of the newspaper are not worth a smile from those who know the truth. It is also said that the merchants in the area will automatically make a statement to prove that there is no such matter.

Declaration of the Chinese Taxpayers Association: The Public Concession Chinese Taxpayers Association declared, "At this time when we are rapidly recovering roads built beyond the boundary and preparing to recover the concession, in order to complete the territorial sovereignty of our great Republic of China, those who oppose the recovery and maintain the status quo, apart from stubborn foreigners, are either those who do not know that there is a country and behave like Jews, or those madmen who rely on strong power to bully those who love peace. According to the Great American Evening Post of this port on August 4 and the North China Daily News on the following day, there is a news report that someone in Western Shanghai has written a letter to the Shanghai Public Concession Municipal Council requesting the expansion of the concession to Western Shanghai. All of us, the masters of the territory, must be shocked and think that those who signed the letter are really people abandoned by the citizens. Moreover, based on their suggestions, they expressed that the Municipal Council has the ability to build, and that the psychology of the residents is expected to have a significant impact. In the view of this association, if you want to make excuses, why worry about no words? This is only a kind of propaganda, which is the intention of those who are not conducive to the integrity of our national sovereignty, and even more so a false action by those who hold aggressive ambitions. If there are Chinese in the list of signatories, if there are responsible Chinese who can represent the residents of Western Shanghai, they will surely treat the letter as a treasure and publicly announce it, thinking that all the special rights that are not allowed by international law are a powerful excuse for not returning them. Otherwise, if they cannot or do not want to present the responsible signatories, then this kind of letter is really like an anonymous posting and has no value. A further presumption is that the writer and the person who sees the letter are both appointed by one party, which is even better, then what impact can this kind of letter have on the psychology of our compatriots? On the contrary, it is enough to prove that roads built beyond the boundary and concessions should be rapidly prepared for recovery, in order to eliminate the delusions of ambitious people. In short, this kind of senseless propaganda is no different from the propaganda of Mao Lisheng's lease of Shanghai on December 7, 1929. It only urges the tension of our country's national rights recovery movement. This declaration is made to reveal the conspiracy. August 5, 1931." The association also sent a letter to the Municipal Council saying, "Dear Sirs, According to the Great American Evening Post of this port on August 4 and the North China Daily News on the following day, there is news that residents of a certain place in Western Shanghai wrote a letter to your office requesting the expansion of the concession to Western Shanghai. We are very surprised. We hereby inquire with your office whether you have received the letter, and if there is such a letter, who are the responsible signatories? This matter is of great importance. We hope you will investigate and reply to us clearly."

Chen Jiliang to Supervise Naval Exercises in Fujian Waters 191

Chen Xunyong Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday

Chen Jiliang, Commander of the First Fleet of the Navy, is about to depart for Sandu in Fujian to supervise naval exercises. The affairs in Shanghai and Hong Kong will be presided over by Chen Xunyong (Zi Daopei), Commander of the Training Fleet, by telegram from the Ministry of the Navy. Chen arrived in Shanghai from Fujian yesterday on the Tongji Training Ship. When the ship passed through Xiangshan, it picked up the Special Battalion of the Naval Guard that had been previously dispatched and returned to Shanghai. In the afternoon, Zheng Zuqing, Secretary of the Training Fleet Command, and Chen Shihui, the aide-de-camp, along with sundries, were also disembarked from the Tongji ship and transported to the Navy Command at Gaochang Temple. As for the First Fleet Commander Chen Jiliang, since someone is in charge, he also ordered the division to prepare yesterday. After receiving the order from the Ministry within a day or two, he will lead eight ships, including Hai Chou, Hai Rong, Yong Jian, Yong Ji, Da Tong, Zi Qiang, Ying Rui, and Tong Ji, to depart for the exercises.

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce

Announces Steps for Dealing with Japanese Goods 193

Present Sacrifices Are for the Survival of Descendants

Economic Severance Should Follow Publicly Agreed Regulations

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce notified various trade associations yesterday, "Dear Sirs, On July 31st, we received a letter from the Anti-Japanese and Aid-Overseas Chinese Committee of all sectors of the city, opening on July 28th, we received a letter from your company, requesting the release of the seized Japanese goods as soon as possible, or transfer them to a warehouse to avoid losses, etc. After checking the case regarding the release of the seized Japanese goods, your association requested a meeting with the association, and it was resolved by the fourth executive committee meeting. The method of disposing of the seized Japanese goods by our association has been published in the newspaper, and a mimeographed copy is attached for your reference. It is hereby notified to you to forward it to your association. After checking the method resolved by the meeting, it is not only related to the transportation industry, and although the above method was sent to the newspapers of this city on July 30th by the association, we are afraid that all industries have not paid close attention to the newspaper reports. We were planning to notify you of the method resolved by the meeting by letter, and we received a letter from the committee stating that we received a letter from you, requesting the return of the goods seized before the 24th, etc. After checking the meeting of the representatives of all sectors of the city, which was held in your council hall on the 13th of this month, it was resolved to permanently sever economic relations with Japan with a calm and extremely courageous spirit. All sectors were represented at the meeting, and there were also many enthusiastic patriotic members of the business community who participated in the meeting on that day. Since the decision was made at the meeting, Japanese goods should not be imported at all. On the 15th, the committee was officially established, and it was also published in the newspaper that all Japanese goods should be stopped from moving. Those who have entered should come to the committee to register. Now the transportation and other industries have not followed the announcement, and have not come to the committee to apply for registration, and have arbitrarily declared the goods for export. This is really inappropriate. However, according to your association's transfer, your association convened a general meeting of members on the 24th of this month and resolved to sever economic relations with Japan and participate in anti-Japanese work. The entire venue unanimously stood up and passed the resolution. Various industries have also successively announced that they will automatically refuse to transport, refuse to load, and refuse to purchase. The voice has been spread, and the whole city is united. After discussion by our association, we all believe that although various industries cannot avoid watching and hesitating in the past, if they can resolutely implement it in the future, showing the true sincerity of the merchants and people in loving the country, and vowing to fight the enemy with the same hatred, it is not too late to mend the fold after the sheep is lost. Therefore, at the fourth executive committee meeting of our association, according to the request of your association and various industries, the method of disposing of Japanese goods was resolved as follows: (A) The disposal of Japanese goods should be divided into three steps: (1) For Japanese goods purchased and stored by merchants before July 14, they should come to the association to register within the registration period. (The registration period ends on August 6, and the registration form should also state: (1) the origin of the goods, (2) the number of the goods, (3) the warehouse where they are stored. After the registration period expires, a certificate will be issued to allow them to be sold without charge. However, if Japanese goods purchased and stored by merchants before July 14 have not been registered and are reported for export and sale, and have been found by our association, a relief fund for anti-Japanese and aid to overseas Chinese will be levied at 10%, and the registration will be supplemented. (2) For Japanese goods purchased and stored by merchants after July 14 and before July 24, if they have not been registered and are reported for export and sale, and have been found by our association, the relief fund for anti-Japanese and aid to overseas Chinese will be doubled, and the registration will be supplemented. (3) After July 24, those who purchase and transport Japanese goods again will be confiscated if found. Even if the goods purchased were before July 24, if they are not registered with the association within the time limit, they will also be confiscated if found. (B) After each item is registered, the respective trade association will collect and store them in one or two warehouses, and send a letter to the association to request the association to send personnel together with the Chamber of Commerce to inspect and verify them clearly. After printing them separately on each item, they will be allowed to be sold for circulation. If they are exported in large quantities, the trade association can send a letter to the association to apply for a pass, which will be stamped and issued by the association together with the Chamber of Commerce for mutual investigation. After the goods arrive, the consignee should first report to the local anti-Japanese association and the Chamber of Commerce for inspection and registration before they can be collected. In the future, if goods are found without stamps, they should be detained and confiscated for use as a relief fund for anti-Japanese and aid to overseas Chinese. The above methods are to be lenient to the past and strict to the future, and to show consideration for the difficulties of merchants while strictly implementing the resistance to goods. We hope that your association will notify various industries to comply with the regulations. As the saying goes, "Cut off the arm when a poisonous snake is in your hand." All of these unavoidable sacrifices at present are for the survival of our descendants for billions of years. We especially hope that your association will sincerely inform them of this. In addition, the goods seized by various industries before the 24th will no longer be replied to one by one. We hope you will check the case and inform them. The so-called "conquering Manchuria and Mongolia in order to conquer the entire China" by the Japanese has long become an open secret in their country, and using Koreans is a precursor to conquering Manchuria and Mongolia. Once this conspiracy is fully completed, how can our people still have a place to eat? The so-called unavoidable sacrifices at present by the association are for the survival of our descendants for billions of years. This is a heart-wrenching and tearful talk. The method of disposing of Japanese goods resolved by the association this time has been changed compared with the first resolution. It is really for the sake of reconciling the spirits of all sectors and cooperating thoroughly. Our business community should especially deeply understand the ancient训 of "The house is falling, the beam is broken, and the beams will be crushed." Understand that the meaning of this economic severance with Japan is completely for self-preservation. With an automatic spirit, abide by publicly agreed regulations, and do not repeat the mistakes of the past with inconsistent steps and divergent opinions.
