Youth Garden

The Garret Room 252

— Ke

Strangely, the term "garret room" in present-day Shanghai can almost be said to have become a specific designation, like "garret room life," "garret room literature." It's like the apartments of Peiping, possessing a unique, mysterious air. However, although I have never lived in one, I always find them unappetizing, even detestable. Needless to say, I have no desire to live in a garret room myself. Even if I see it mentioned in print or hear it in conversation, the phrase "garret room" immediately gives me a gray feeling—narrowness, disorder, air that is humid and musty, a listless, pale face, disheveled hair, a drooping head, a hunched back, withered and disappointed eyes. These things flash like a movie before my eyes, arousing my discomfort.

I remember one day I actually went into a garret room, but the impression I got was not at all what I imagined—and the unpleasantness was even more profound.

That day, it was just the weather for wearing velvet robes. Qin changed into a newly made velvet cheongsam and hurried to my room, asking me to accompany her to Jiangwan to see a friend.

"Where does he live?" I asked.

"A garret room," she said.

"Oh, a garret room." Narrowness, disorder… flashed through my brain again like lightning.

"I'm not going," I said.

"What? Not going? He's a good friend, please, come with me."

I was dragged and pulled by her until I finally agreed to go with her. We got off the train, took a rickshaw, and turned several corners.

"We're here," Qin said, and the rickshaw stopped.

"Garden Street No. ×××." I glanced at the house number and followed Qin through the gate. I don't remember how, but we turned a corner, and a staircase suddenly blocked our path. We went up the stairs. Qin said in a low voice,

"Look, that's the room."

Nailed to the door of the room on the left were two torn business cards. From the room came the sound of "pat, pat" mahjong tiles, mixed with a gentle, slightly flirtatious laughter. Qin gently knocked on the door a few times.

"Who is it? Come in," followed by the door creaking open.

"Helloooooo…"

"Heyyyyy…"

About five or six men and women inside rushed to greet Qin, and I followed her into the room. I suddenly felt cramped and uneasy and almost wanted to retreat.

Qin introduced me to everyone one by one. I just nodded slightly to everyone, standing unnaturally behind Qin.

"Please sit down," Qin's friend Xiaolan said very politely. He was a man with small eyes and a pointed face, wearing a celery-green silk lined robe, and suit pants dragging behind his heels.

"Uh," I responded in my nose, and sat down on a chair near the door.

Next to the chair were a lot of things piled up messily—a kerosene stove, with a tilted lead pot on top. In the pot, muddy water soaked a few spoons. A lead bucket, a tin kettle, a vegetable bowl, with a few pairs of chopsticks resting on top. I carefully positioned my feet, afraid of touching black soot or knocking something over.

"Sorry for disturbing your mahjong game," Qin said with a mocking smile.

"It's nothing," Xiaolan seemed to understand and explained, "This is just for relaxation, entertainment, leisure after class, it's nothing."

……………………………………

A girl with big eyes and high cheekbones was sitting at the head of the mahjong table, on a small iron bed covered with a blackish-gray (originally white) blanket. She glanced at Xiaolan, smiled at a man with a Cantonese accent sitting on her right, and tilted her head down to his shoulder. She deftly made a cylinder with her fingers, pressed it tightly against the man's left ear, pressed her blood-red thick lips against the edge of her thumb, and whispered to him. The man also smiled at Xiaolan.

Opposite the room were two small iron beds, which were the masters of Xiaolan and the Cantonese man. The Cantonese man had a tall figure, a dark face. What made him most recognizable was his big nose, which was a little disproportionate.

"Xiu, sing a song," said a man with a local accent, short and neatly dressed in a suit, to the girl standing by the window turning the pages of a songbook, while dragging the phonograph on the stool in front of him. "Falling Flowers and Flowing Water," is this the one? As he spoke, he started it up.

"No, who wants to sing this?" Xiu tilted her head slightly, but finally walked to the phonograph and sang in a high-pitched tone along with the record. She was very fair-skinned, and there were a few freckles on her round face, but they didn't make her look ugly. She had a nimble figure, often liked to prop her hand on her waist, which made her look even more graceful.

The singing interrupted Qin and Xiaolan's conversation.

"Sorry to neglect our new guest, this place is very messy," Xiaolan suddenly said to me humbly.

"No...this house is very clean," my voice was so low that I could barely hear myself.

"She, she likes silence," Qin said, turning around and smiling at me.

"Yes, diligent people always love silence," Xiaolan shrugged.

I smiled and said nothing.

"Xiaofeng, she doesn't like to talk much, do you understand?" Qin said, looking at me teasingly again.

"Haha…" Xiaolan laughed loudly.

"What is this, so annoying?" I thought.

Indeed, at this time I felt a kind of contempt, disgust, and wished I could run out immediately.

"If there's nothing else, we can go," I stood up and asked Qin.

"Go back? Anyway, there's nothing important, let's talk a bit more," Qin objected.

"Then, I'll go first, you can talk more," I resolutely said goodbye to them. They casually said a few words to persuade me to stay, and then sent me to the door. I vaguely heard them say,

"Her appearance is amiable, but her temperament is too aloof."

Then there was the sound of "pat, pat" of the mahjong tiles and teasing laughter again.

This was more than a year ago. Contempt and disgust still float in my mind.

When I left school this summer vacation, Lin asked me,

"What are you planning to do during this long vacation?"

"I really want to write something, but the place is too noisy," I said.

"You can do this, rent another garret room, just you alone, wouldn't it be very quiet?"

"Alas, how can I?" I shook my head and answered her. I knew very well that apart from studying, I wouldn't do anything else. I can't make a pot of edible rice with just the right amount of water, or pick up a basket to go to the market to buy some fish, meat, or vegetables. I can't do anything, so how can I be qualified to live in a garret room? But now I am really sitting in a garret room, and all day long.

It's been a week since I came back to my sister's place, and I can't read or write anything. My sister, she loves to gossip the most. The two nieces are lively and naughty. There are children crying in the front neighbor's house, and the neighbor on the left is playing mahjong and fighting. "I'm not afraid of these," I made a firm decision. I'll try to do things. When I pick up the pen, all I hear is "wa, wa wa…" "pat, crack," and only these complex sounds are fluctuating in my brain, and under the pen I can't help but repeatedly write these few words. "Let's change the taste," I went to get a book to read again, but on the pages, the rows of black words are clearly written, but I can't understand anything inside. "What to do, if this continues, it's really terrible," I was anxious all day, wanting to get a quieter place.

"A garret room, just you alone, wouldn't it be very quiet?" Lin's words suddenly repeated in my consciousness again, arousing my attention to the garret room at my sister's place.

The door of this room opens onto the sun deck. We have never gone inside. Last year, the amah lived there. This year, the amah moved downstairs, and it was just used to store things, boxes, wooden buckets, tin boxes, bamboo baskets… messily filled the room. Although the inside is not very big, it is very quiet. If you close the door on the sun deck and the door leading to the wing room, not a single bit of the noisy sounds outside will get in. So I started to clean up, stacked more than a dozen boxes into three piles, and arranged them against the wall in a row. I put a square table by the window, with a few useful books and ink, etc. Under the table, I just piled up some odds and ends of waste. The wooden buckets and tin boxes… were all slightly tidied up and stacked in the corner of the wall by the window.

"Oh, what an elaborate writing room," my sister said mockingly, but I thought the light was very good and was very satisfied.

The window faces the back gate of a government office, and the air is still fresh. A plane tree is planted at the back gate of the government office, and the dense green shade covers the entire alley in cool shade. When a gentle breeze blows, the leaves often make a rustling sound, giving people a light and happy feeling. At first, the room was a bit moldy, but later, after my diligent cleaning, it became very refreshing. After washing up every day, I sit at the square table by the window, quietly savoring the life of the garret room. No matter how noisy it is outside, it cannot move the strings of my silent heart. However, there is one annoying thing, the windows and doors on the second floor of the government office face each other, and the clerks inside often deliberately cough loudly during their leisure time, shush, shush...

Javelin Throw 253

— Bing She

Shanghai Market

Business News 254

The Marty Motor Company announces that, for the convenience of residents in the western district to purchase cars, the company has prepared to establish a Global Motor Company at the corner of Jing'an Temple Road and Muir Road, to serve as a new showroom. In addition to distributing the American Austin cars, it will also sell Chrysler DeSoto six-cylinder and eight-cylinder cars. The new showroom is now ready and will open soon. All circles are welcome to visit.

The Tianmu Weiya Bamboo Shoots Company announces that bamboo shoots, also known as flattened tips, are a specialty of Zhejiang, and those produced in Tianmu Mountain are especially known as valuable. Because they get the beauty of the mountains and rivers, and nurture the essence of heaven and earth, the annual output is rare, and rarely reaches Shanghai. Now, Mr. Zhou Yifan, a Zhejiang businessman, has raised funds to establish this company in Juxing Lane, Beidi Road, in the French Concession, with the two characters "Tianmu" as the trademark. At the foot of Tianmu Mountain in Zhejiang, land is expanded to plant bamboo. After the bamboo shoots are harvested, scientific methods are used to set up factories to select and manufacture them. All products are tender, fresh, clean and hygienic, and the decoration is beautiful, which is different from the ordinary. It is suitable for family meals and gifts to relatives and friends, and the price is very cheap. The major companies in this port, such as Sincere, Wing On, Sun Sun, Lihua, and Guanshengyuan, are their managers. Gourmets can try to buy from the above-mentioned places, and they will be able to satisfy their appetites.

The Peide Tie Company announces that the company has newly released a type A No. 5 electric woven striped satin tie with more than twenty kinds of colors. The exquisiteness of the product is superior to that of imported products, and a price list and samples are printed. Send a letter and it will be sent immediately.

The Xihua Glasses Company at the intersection of North Sichuan Road and West Wuchang Road announces that the company has been open for many years, and its business is developed, with high quality and low prices. The appointment period is free of errors. Newly arrived various European and American platinum and red gold high-end frames are strong, exquisite, and fairly priced, which are highly praised by all circles, and sales are also large.

The Datong Traditional Chinese Medicine Store in Jialu Road announces that the market in Jialu Road, French Concession, is becoming increasingly prosperous, but large-scale pharmacies are still lacking, which is a pity for the general residents. Recently, Mr. Xu Jianshan, a well-known real estate owner, has noticed this and created this pharmacy for the convenience of the residents. Ginseng and all kinds of medicinal pills are made by expert Xu Zhengang, which is truly for the happiness of the public and is very different from those who seek profit. It will be officially opened on August 3rd of the lunar calendar, and the local residents will benefit greatly.

The Kaiming Bookstore in Fuzhou Road announces that the store has been working hard in the publishing business in recent years. The new books published are no less than four or five hundred kinds. Recently, it has compiled and printed middle school textbooks and worked hard in education as the leader in the new book industry. It has established branches in Guangzhou, Peiping, Shenyang, etc., and has considerable authority in the publishing industry. Recently, in order to facilitate readers in Hubei Province, the store will set up a branch in Hankou. It has already leased No. 15 Jincheng Lane, Hubei Street, Hankou, and the arrangements have been made. It will open on August 11th, and there will be a lively event at that time.

Theater News 255

The Datong Film Company announces that the company's first group, Shangwu Detective's new film "The Legend of the Heroic Hero," directed by Wang Fuqing, has been proceeding smoothly for days. Regarding the official name of the film, the company's production meeting has decided to name it "Three Keys." The starting point of the play is based on the key. Although it has gone through some storms, it has finally regained the beauty because of the key. Although the key is a small object, it controls the entire film, so the naming is very new and appropriate. In addition, the company's second group, Ding Xing's new comedy film "The Light of the Peddler," is a film for ordinary people, and the production is also very satisfactory.

The Tianyi Film Company announces that the company has spent a lot of money to purchase the Movietone machine for producing sound films and hired professional talents to actively proceed, which is likely to lead the Chinese film industry. Recently, it has purchased a five-color camera from the United States for shooting five-color sound films. The films shot by the item camera are based on chemical action, and all colors are the same as the real thing, which is completely different from dyeing. It has been transported to Shanghai yesterday. In the future, when the item five-color sound film is made, it will be a new experience for the audience.

Calligraphy and Painting News 256

The Youzheng Bookstore announces that General Wangsun Puyuan, named Tong, is the first celebrity of the Qing imperial family. His calligraphy, painting, poetry, and songs were famous for a time. He is currently a teacher at Tsinghua University. He is visiting Shanghai during the summer vacation. He has painted various kinds of Buddha pagodas, including the Heart Sutra, the Immeasurable Life Sutra, the Amitabha Sutra, and the Universal Gate Sutra. He uses high-quality materials from the internal treasury and draws the Buddha statues solemnly on magnetic blue paper with real mud gold. The font is extraordinary and is displayed in the Youzheng Bookstore for a reduced price of sixty to eighty yuan. The mounting is exquisite, making it the best gift for birthday celebrations. Those who need it should not miss it.

Yang Zhiyi Medical Office, No. 89 Pingle Lane, Xizang Road, announces that this medical doctor specializes in the treatment of lung and kidney diseases. All symptoms of cough, hemoptysis, spermatorrhea, and leucorrhea will be cured once treated. Recently, due to the hot weather, patients who come from afar suffer unspeakable hardships when running around to see a doctor in the hot sun. A night clinic has been specially added, scheduled from 8:00 to 10:00 every night, to benefit patients.

Social News

New York Working Women's Life (10) 259

— Lin

The daily life of a woman earning thirty to forty dollars a week, our friend A'Dai'er Lan Bao, is as follows:

The clock strikes eight, A'Dai'er stretches, still curled up in the comfortable warmth of her quilt. She feels a little ache in her legs, but soon forgets it.

A'Dai'er works as a model in a clothing wholesaler. She lives in a shared apartment. The landlords are a young couple who rent out the extra rooms to reduce their huge expenses. A'Dai'er has freedom to come and go. She uses the apartment for socialising, which greatly frustrates the landlords. A'Dai'er pays ten dollars a week for rent. The room is simply furnished, although she has added a few knotted pillows, three French dolls, and several Maxfield Parrish prints.

A'Dai'er originally came to New York to pursue a career on stage. In fact, she spent four weeks in theatre, selected for a musical troupe. She was carefree and very happy. The rehearsal period lasted a month, during which the actors were of course not paid. Then they performed for three days in a small theater in the suburbs, before returning for another week of rehearsals. This final week also had no pay. Finally, the troupe performed at a theatre in New York, but after three weeks of poor business, it closed. A'Dai'er felt that a life in theatre was too unstable for her financial situation. She found a new position as a model in a clothing store. This job was long and mentally tiring, but the wages were reliable. A'Dai'er initially earned thirty dollars a week, but later found another position paying thirty-five dollars a week.

Getting up in the morning is truly painful. This is the busiest time for clothing wholesalers. How much A'Dai'er would like to sleep until noon. She jumps out of bed, takes a bath, and gets dressed – the procedure is very simple.

A'Dai'er goes to a cheap restaurant for breakfast. This restaurant is on Broadway. She needs to eat something to sustain her through the morning's work, because she has learned from experience that she is prone to fainting if she doesn't eat.

It doesn't matter if she is five or ten minutes late for work, unless it becomes a habit. She usually arrives at the clothing store at a quarter past nine.

In the clothing wholesale store, models are treated like business supplies. These women wear thin undershirts and short, tight-fitting camisoles, so that the clothes fit well. If they are not busy, they sit in the storage room in their camisoles, and when they feel cold and bored, they can smoke a cigarette to relieve their boredom. Although they wear very little clothing, no one pays them much attention. When buyers come in, the models must try on various clothes for them to see. There is a special skill to wearing clothes. A'Dai'er's limited stage experience helps a lot, because she knows how to handle her figure. Each piece of clothing must be put on and taken off, taken off and put on. The models should always look happy and cheerful. Sometimes, salespeople behave rudely or insultingly towards the models. The girls have to ignore it completely.

A'Dai'er often helps to sell clothes. Perhaps one day she will sell them herself, although she does not yet have sufficient experience to do so. Moreover, she feels unstable and lacks a sense of responsibility. She knows that one day she will get married. She is currently quite satisfied with her lifestyle.

The clothes she wears as samples are specially made for her, so they fit perfectly. She walks back and forth in the clothes. It is truly a hard and laborious task, but she makes it look happy and joyful. When the salesperson places a large order for the clothes she is wearing, the manager pats her back to indicate approval.

This particular morning, the store is very busy. Many out-of-town customers are gathered inside. The girls have to work twice as fast. Several people are waiting in the dressing room to help them put on and take off clothes. The manager walks in and says, "Girls, you only have half an hour for lunch today. We need to show all the clothes to four major buyers. Make sure you are not late."

The girls don't show obvious satisfaction with this announcement. "Ah, that's unlucky, who do you think I am, your slave?" Similar curses are muttered behind the manager's back, but all the girls return to the store on time. They run to a nearby diner and eat some hot sandwiches and steamed buns, etc. This menu is slightly different from usual, because the girls pay close attention to their diet. If they gain weight, their positions will be in jeopardy. During the meal, they talk a lot about the work situation. These girls are all very familiar with each other, so they speak without reservation. They know nothing of outward modesty.

The afternoon continues to be hectic. It's not until a quarter past six that A'Dai'er wearily puts on her own clothes. The manager walks out and says to her, "A'Dai'er, I want to see you." She buttons up her clothes and runs to the manager's office.

"Listen carefully, child, that buyer from Hawaii is a really good man. He wants to take you out for dinner and a show. Now listen carefully, he is a good man, otherwise I wouldn't let you go."

A'Dai'er knows that the manager wants to make a big deal with this buyer tomorrow. She already has an appointment for tonight and doesn't want to change it, but she understands that business is important.

"Okay, I will definitely go, but Jack, you have to give me a dress to wear here. I can't wear my own tattered clothes, and there isn't enough time to go home and change."

Many girls call the manager by his first name. At this moment, Jack frowns, because there is an unwritten rule that models cannot wear clothes from the store outside. Sometimes girls violate this rule, and if it is discovered, they will be fired. Jack feels that A'Dai'er is deliberately blackmailing him, but he eventually agrees.

"Okay, A'Dai'er, do it that way, but don't let the other girls know."

In clothing wholesale stores, models have a privilege. They can buy any nice clothes at a very low price. They can buy sample clothes in bulk. If the season has passed, when the wholesale period has passed but retail sales are still ongoing, this agreement is mutually beneficial. If a woman works as a model in a clothing store, and her boss often deals with wholesale stores, she can have her choose clothes from the wholesale store.

While the other girls hurry home, A'Dai'er lingers in the store. She begins to dress very carefully. She knows that Jack would not ask her to entertain the buyer if he were unreliable. Many buyers think they have a privilege to socialize with the models at any time. In lower-level wholesale stores, they consider this one of the model's duties, requiring them to entertain out-of-town buyers. In this particular situation, A'Dai'er knows that the buyer from Hawaii might be lonely in New York and wants a companion for entertainment.

She chooses a green dress that the buyer had greatly admired. She wants to show off this dress to him for a night, and maybe he will order it.

The hotel where they are to meet is only four blocks from the store. A'Dai'er hires a car and sits inside comfortably, but only for a short time. She tells the driver to wait for her, and then tells the buyer that she has hired a car outside, because hiring a car is very difficult at this time of night. Even if she knew someone was really rich, A'Dai'er would never call him to spend his money. She knows a young man studying law. When he takes her out, she always suggests going to places that don't cost much money. They go to the movies or take the subway. But when meeting this major buyer, she will never do that.

He has already prepared for the night's entertainment, even booking a dinner. They dine on the rooftop of a large hotel in the theatre district. This place is rarely open in winter. A lavish dinner is displayed on the table, complete with everything from oysters and cheese to biscuits. A'Dai'er tastes a little of everything, while the buyer eats a lot of everything. They are often silent, except when discussing the clothing business. A'Dai'er knows she should be lively and tell some jokes, but there are no fresh incidents.

"Let's go see a new play." As they walk out of the hotel's main entrance into the car, the buyer says eagerly, but when he mentions the name of the play, A'Dai'er's heart sinks. However, she soon recovers her cheerful appearance. In fact, she has seen this great opera at least eight times with different buyers, as if they all love to see this show. Of course, they never ask the models what shows they like. The buyers see them as mere tools, not as human women.

During the conversation, they don't only talk about the wholesale store where A'Dai'er works. The buyer has asked her several questions about styles, and seems to value her opinion very seriously. For A'Dai'er, this evening is truly unbearable. For the buyer, it's just seeing the sights of New York. He will go back and tell his roommates about the beautiful girl he escorted in New York, and the considerable amount of money he spent that night. He will also warn them not to mention it in front of his wife.

A'Dai'er can recite the plot of the play by heart. She is just as familiar with the costumes and music. She gradually feels sleepy. She struggles to fight off sleep, trying not to doze off in her fatigue. During the performance, she even points out how wonderful the play is, to please her companion.

She longs to go home to sleep and rest her aching body. After the play, there is nothing else to do. They go to a popular nightclub for dancing and snacks. A'Dai'er is slightly reluctant, but eventually gives in. At the nightclub, they wear low hats, blow whistles, dance, and eat until three o'clock. Afterwards, everyone is exhausted. She tells the out-of-town buyer how delightful the evening was. She is so tired that she collapses onto her bed and falls asleep immediately. (To be continued)
